# What's new ‚Äî CityAgent Analytics

Hybrid feature changelog (our additions on top of the bagofwords/Dash base). Newest first.
Format per entry: `## v<semver> ‚Äî <title>  (<YYYY-MM-DD>)` then bullets.

## v1.160.0 ‚Äî Julius-quality output: show-your-work notebook, data-aware follow-ups, smarter charts & starters (Phase 4)  (2026-07-07)
- **Analysis notebook** ‚Äî a step-by-step "show your work" trail of how an answer was reached (what each step did + its result), like Julius. Read-only, built from the analysis steps already saved. Turn on **Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí Analysis Notebook**.
- **Data-aware follow-ups** ‚Äî suggested next questions now reference the real columns and example values from your result, not just re-word the answer. Turn on **Data-aware Follow-ups** (needs Follow-ups on).
- **Smarter charts** ‚Äî the automatic chart picker now also catches: empty result ‚Üí table, a single number ‚Üí KPI card, a date + a measure ‚Üí trend line, two dimensions + a measure ‚Üí heatmap. Turn on **Smart Viz Picker**.
- **Data-grounded starters** ‚Äî the sample questions on an agent now name concrete segments/periods your data actually contains. Turn on **Data-grounded Starters**.
  - 4 new flags (3-place, category Intelligence, all default OFF, byte-identical when off): `HYBRID_ANALYSIS_NOTEBOOK`, `HYBRID_FOLLOWUPS_DATA_AWARE`, `HYBRID_STARTERS_DATA_GROUNDED`; `HYBRID_SMART_VIZ` (pre-existing) broadened. Built by 3 disjoint-file subagents; flags added up-front to avoid a hybrid_flags.py race.
  - NEW `ai/knowledge/notebook.py::build_analysis_notebook(db, *, report_id, completion_id=None)` ‚Äî loads Steps via `Widget.report_id` join, per-step `{title, did, result, chart}` (result via `sense_maker._df_from_step_data` + `compute_insights`, no raw code, no LLM), fail-soft ‚Üí None when off. Endpoint `GET /api/reports/{report_id}/notebook` on `report_slides.py` (sibling auth/org-scope; returns `{enabled:false}` when off).
  - `ai/knowledge/followups.py` ‚Äî `_build_prompt`/`generate_followups` gained optional `result_columns`; NEW `_recent_result_columns` pulls the latest tabular step's columns (name/dtype/samples) when `FOLLOWUPS_DATA_AWARE` on. `create_data.py::_smart_viz_override` ‚Äî 4 new deterministic rules (all check `ALLOWED_VIZ_TYPES`, fail-soft). `data_source.py::generate_conversation_starters` ‚Äî injects sampled `values=` from the schema when `STARTERS_DATA_GROUNDED` on.
  - Verified live org b2bec83d: flags 3-place default OFF; smart-viz 0-rows‚Üítable + 1-value‚Üímetric_card; notebook built report b23b407d (1 step "Average Cans Per Month ‚Üí 1 row √ó 1 column"); data-aware followups pulled real column `avg_cans_per_month float64 e.g. 1.54`. Endpoints 401 (registered+auth). Hot-cp'd into `:dev`, then baked.

## v1.159.0 ‚Äî Reusing a proven query now understands paraphrased questions (Phase 3b accuracy)  (2026-07-07)
- When you ask something in different words than last time ("revenue per month" vs "monthly sales total"), the agent now still finds and reuses the right proven query it learned earlier. It ranks past queries by both wording overlap AND meaning (embeddings), and your golden queries still win ties. Off by default ‚Äî turn on **Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí Learned-query recall (embedding + RRF)**.
  - New flag `HYBRID_RECALL_RRF` (3-place, category Accuracy, default OFF). Recall (`ai/knowledge/query_learning.py::recall_learned_queries`) gained an optional `organization` arg (for the embeddings provider) and a flag-gated branch that fuses the Jaccard rank with an embedding-cosine rank via Reciprocal Rank Fusion (`_rrf_rerank`, k=60, golden tiebreak, cosine-floor 0.35 noise filter).
  - No embedding column exists on `query_library_items`, so candidate vectors are computed on the fly in one batched `embeddings.embed_texts` call (the approved recall set is small). Fully fail-soft: no provider / empty vectors ‚Üí `None` ‚Üí the original pure-Jaccard ranking, so the prompt is byte-identical when the flag is off. `coder.py` recall call now passes `organization=_org`.
  - Verified: pure helpers (`_cosine`/`_rank_map`/`_rrf_rerank`) + flag 3-place + fallback-to-Jaccard on no-vectors (stubbed). Live on org b2bec83d (26 approved rows / 2 data sources): real OpenRouter embeddings HTTP 200, RRF re-ranked vs Jaccard (rank-3 flipped "Avg Consumption by Brand" ‚Üí "Avg Consumption by SKU"), both clean, no error.

## v1.158.0 ‚Äî The code generator now sees defined joins, metric formulas, and column meanings (Phase 3 accuracy)  (2026-07-07)
- The part that writes the query now receives the business grounding it used to guess at: your approved column meanings, metric formulas, and known table joins ‚Äî scoped to the tables it's working with ‚Äî so it uses your definitions instead of inventing join keys or re-deriving a metric. Previously that knowledge reached only the planning step, not the code writer. Off by default ‚Äî turn on **Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí Coder grounding (semantic + metrics + joins)** (needs the Semantic layer / Metrics catalog / Join graph layers you already have).
  - New flag `HYBRID_CODER_GROUNDING` (3-place, category Accuracy, default OFF). New `CodeGenContext.grounding_context` field (seam).
  - NEW `ai/agents/coder/grounding.py::build_grounding_context` ‚Äî reuses the existing APPROVED-ONLY builders (`SemanticContextBuilder`, `MetricsContextBuilder`, `JoinGraphContextBuilder`), scopes each to the coder's target tables (normalized name match) and ranks by the question, renders a compact block (Column meanings / Metric formulas verbatim / Known joins), hard-capped ~6000 chars, fully fail-soft (any error ‚Üí "").
  - `prompt_formatters.py::build_codegen_context` populates `grounding_context` (fail-soft, from `runtime_ctx` db/org + `tables_by_source`). `coder.py::generate_code` renders it before the pushdown block with "use these EXACTLY ‚Äî do NOT invent join keys or re-derive a defined metric."
  - Subsections inherit their layer flags (SEMANTIC_LAYER / METRICS_CATALOG / JOIN_GRAPH, all default ON) ‚Äî block is empty if those have no approved rows. Byte-identical prompt when `CODER_GROUNDING` off or nothing approved. Verified: flag-off ‚Üí "" in-container; flag-on with real org data ‚Üí 3271-char grounding block (column meanings + metric formulas + joins, approved-only).

## v1.157.1 ‚Äî Fix: DuckDB-over-file analysis no longer false-crashes on the memory cap  (2026-07-07)
- Caught in local smoke-testing before AWS: the isolated sandbox's per-run memory cap was rejecting DuckDB queries as "out of memory" even on tiny data. Root cause ‚Äî the cap limited *virtual* address space (`RLIMIT_AS`), and DuckDB/pyarrow reserve large virtual space up front regardless of data size, so a 2 GB cap tripped on a 28k-row GROUP BY. The one-shot child's real memory protection is the container memory limit + the fact that all its memory is freed the instant it exits + the run timeout ‚Äî none of which false-trip. So the child now defaults to NO virtual cap and relies on those. This unblocks the new DuckDB-over-file upload path.
  - `code_execution.py`: new `_resolve_subprocess_mem_cap_mb()` (default 0 = no `RLIMIT_AS`; opt-in hard virtual ceiling via `SANDBOX_SUBPROCESS_MEM_MB`, ‚â•4096 recommended if used). Subprocess dispatch now uses it instead of forcing `DEFAULT_SANDBOX_MEM_LIMIT_MB` (2048) ‚Äî which was the false-trip. In-process path + its `SANDBOX_MEM_LIMIT_MB` knob unchanged. Verified: DuckDB `read_csv_auto` GROUP BY top-3 over 28k rows runs clean in the one-shot child at the new default, returns only the 3 aggregated rows.

## v1.157.0 ‚Äî Uploaded-file questions run in the database + generated SQL is checked before it runs (Phase 2)  (2026-07-07)
- Two speed/accuracy wins, both off by default. (1) When you ask a summary/total/top-N about an uploaded file, the answer is now computed inside a fast query engine (DuckDB) over the file instead of loading the whole file into memory and crunching it afterward ‚Äî same answer, far less memory, closer to how the fastest tools work. (2) The system now sanity-checks the query it wrote before running it and, if a run fails, tells itself exactly what was wrong with the SQL so the retry fixes it ‚Äî fewer "An error occurred" dead-ends. Turn on **Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí SQL pushdown (memory discipline)** and **SQL dry-plan validation**.
  - **DuckDB-over-file (part of `HYBRID_SANDBOX_PUSHDOWN`, prompt-only):** `agents/coder/coder.py` ‚Äî the pushdown block now makes `duckdb.query("‚Ä¶ FROM read_csv_auto('<path>') GROUP BY ‚Ä¶ LIMIT ‚Ä¶").to_df()` the DEFAULT for uploaded-file aggregate/top-N/count/filter questions (with a concrete worked example), plus an explicit anti-pattern line against `SELECT *`/whole-file-then-pandas. The "return granular rows / do not pre-aggregate" exception was moved to the TOP so it still wins. `duckdb` confirmed allowed by the sandbox AST gate (not in `FORBIDDEN_MODULES`). Byte-identical prompt when the flag is OFF.
  - **SQL dry-plan validation (`HYBRID_SQL_VALIDATE`, new flag, 3-place, default OFF):** NEW `ai/code_execution/sql_validate.py` ‚Äî `validate_sql()` parses generated SQL with `sqlglot` (read-only via 'duckdb' dialect), flags write/DDL (INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE/DROP/‚Ä¶) and a mild `SELECT *`-without-LIMIT advisory; `build_sql_error_feedback()` composes a structured hint. Wired into BOTH retry loops in `code_execution.py` (`generate_and_execute_stream` v1 + `_v2`): on a failed run the offending SQL's diagnosis is appended to the corrective feedback fed back to the model, so the regeneration is targeted. Fully fail-soft ‚Äî sqlglot missing / parse-uncertain / any error ‚Üí allow (no-op). `sqlglot==30.7.0` added to `requirements_versioned.txt` (pure-python; flag is a no-op until it's in the image).
  - Verified: good SELECT allowed; DROP/DELETE blocked with read-only hint; unparseable SQL ‚Üí parse-fail hint; `SELECT *` ‚Üí advisory only; pure no-op when sqlglot absent. All four touched files compile; byte-identical when both flags OFF.

## v1.156.0 ‚Äî Isolated sandbox is now safe for live databases (query log, quota, read-only restored)  (2026-07-07)
- When a live-database question runs in the isolated sandbox, the executed SQL now shows up in the query log again, usage/quota metering still counts it, and the read-only safety check still blocks any accidental write ‚Äî the same protections the normal path already had. This closes the gap that previously made "Subprocess sandbox ‚Äî live DB clients" unsafe to turn on. The base uploaded-file sandbox is unchanged and remains the recommended first switch.
  - `subprocess_pool.py`: new `_ChildQueryCapture` proxy wraps each rebuilt live client IN THE CHILD ‚Äî enforces the read-only string guard (`_enforce_readonly_query`, lazy-imported at child runtime, gated on `READONLY_ENFORCE`) before every `execute_query`, and records `{sql, query_ms, rows, result_bytes, connection_id}` per query. `_rebuild_clients` now takes shared capture lists; `_worker` sends `captured_queries`/`captured_timings` on every result path (success/spill/error); `SandboxResult` carries them back.
  - `code_execution.py`: the offload return path now MERGES the child-captured queries + timings into the caller's `executed_queries`/`captured_timings` (were empty before) and calls new `_replay_subprocess_quota()` ‚Äî the parent owns the DB/usage_context, so it re-consumes query + data-bytes quota from the child's recorded metadata. Fail-soft: quotas off / no connection_id / any error ‚Üí no-op. Orgs without QUOTAS unaffected.
  - Deterministic memory pool: `_resolve_max_concurrency()` makes the sandbox concurrency env-tunable (`HYBRID_SANDBOX_MAX_CONCURRENCY`, default cpus-2) ‚Äî worst-case pool memory = `max_concurrency √ó per-child mem_mb`; keep that under the box's cgroup `mem_limit` and excess runs QUEUE instead of over-committing. Still NOT wired to warehouse result-cache in the child (cache lives in the parent process) ‚Äî documented, deferred.
  - All flag-gated + reversible; byte-identical when `SUBPROCESS_SANDBOX` off. Verified: capture records rows/bytes/conn, read-only guard blocks `DROP` (never reaches client), delegation + concurrency-tunable pass.

## v1.155.0 ‚Äî Lighter runs: let the database do the heavy lifting (Phase 5)  (2026-07-07)
- Analysis runs now use far less memory by pushing filtering and totals down to the database and pulling only the rows the answer needs ‚Äî instead of loading whole tables into memory and filtering afterward. Same answers, smaller footprint ‚Üí more questions run at once on the same box. Off by default ‚Äî turn on **Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí SQL pushdown (memory discipline)**.
  - BE flag `HYBRID_SANDBOX_PUSHDOWN` (3-place, Performance, default OFF). `agents/coder/coder.py`: `generate_code` builds a flag-gated `pushdown_block` (empty when OFF) injected after the data-granularity rule ‚Äî tells the model to put WHERE/GROUP BY/aggregate/LIMIT in the SQL (not `SELECT *` then filter in pandas), return already-aggregated results for summaries, and read large uploaded files via DuckDB SQL (`read_csv_auto`) instead of whole-file `pd.read_csv`. Explicitly defers to the existing "return granular rows / do not pre-aggregate" directive so it never overrides it.
  - Prompt-only, reversible; no code-path change. Pairs with the subprocess sandbox (v1.153/1.154): pushdown shrinks each run so fewer hit the per-child memory cap and more fit per box. Phase 6 (separate exec container at ~300+ users) still to come.

## v1.154.0 ‚Äî Isolated sandbox now covers live-database analysis too (Phase 4)  (2026-07-07)
- The isolated-process sandbox (from the last release) now also covers questions that query a **live SQL database** (Postgres, MySQL, Snowflake, etc.), not just uploaded files ‚Äî so those runs free their memory on exit too. Cloud/BI connectors (Power BI, Fabric, OneDrive, SharePoint) still run the current way. Off by default ‚Äî turn on **Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí Subprocess sandbox ‚Äî live DB clients** (needs the base Subprocess sandbox flag on).
  - BE flag `HYBRID_SUBPROCESS_SANDBOX_LIVE` (3-place, Performance, default OFF; requires `HYBRID_SUBPROCESS_SANDBOX`). `data_source_service.construct_clients`/`construct_client` stamp a serializable `client._build_spec = {type, params}` (exact ctor kwargs incl. decrypted creds) on each built client. `subprocess_pool._rebuild_clients` reconstructs plain-SQL clients IN THE CHILD via `resolve_client_class(type)(**params)` (no DB), reapplies driver-level read-only when `READONLY_ENFORCE` is on, wraps in the tolerant `ClientResolver`. `_worker` runs `generate_df(db_clients, excel_files)`; a rebuild miss returns `rebuild_failed` ‚Üí the caller falls back in-process (never a hard fail).
  - `code_execution.py`: `_subprocess_offload_plan` returns None (in-process) / `{}` (upload) / `{key: spec}` (live). Live path gated by the sub-flag + `_SUBPROCESS_LIVE_TYPES` allowlist (OAuth/BI/file connectors excluded) + all clients carrying a spec; loadables/http/federate/input_df always stay in-process. Write/DDL SQL is already rejected by the parent AST guard before dispatch, so it never reaches the child; the child also reapplies driver read-only. In-child SQL isn't captured into `executed_queries` (the answer/df is unaffected).
  - Verified in-container: a live Postgres `SELECT` returns identical results with the live flag OFF (in-process) vs ON (child rebuilds the client, queries ca-postgres). Non-allowlisted/OAuth clients ‚Üí in-process. Phase 5 (DuckDB pushdown + row caps) and Phase 6 (separate exec container) still to come. Not baked into the image; flag OFF = today's behavior.

## v1.153.0 ‚Äî Isolated sandbox: uploaded-file analysis no longer fills memory  (2026-07-07)
- Analyzing an uploaded file now runs in its **own throwaway process** ‚Äî all its memory is released the moment it finishes, instead of piling up in the shared server and eventually making the box unhealthy. A single heavy or runaway run can no longer slow down or crash everyone else's; it hits its own memory/time limit and stops cleanly. Off by default ‚Äî turn on **Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí Subprocess sandbox**.
  - BE flag `HYBRID_SUBPROCESS_SANDBOX` (3-place, Performance, default OFF). NEW `ai/code_execution/subprocess_pool.py`: `run_local_code(...)` runs already-AST-vetted code in a one-shot `forkserver` child (pandas/numpy preloaded ‚Üí ~ms start), bounded by a `BoundedSemaphore(cpu-2)`, per-child `RLIMIT_AS`/`RLIMIT_CPU`/`RLIMIT_FSIZE` (now safe = per-process) + wall-clock `SIGKILL`; result returned as parquet bytes (spills to disk >50MB). Memory reclaimed on child exit.
  - `code_execution.py`: `execute_code` dispatches to the pool **only** for upload-only runs (`_can_offload_to_subprocess`: flag ON, files present, NO live DB clients / loadables / http / federate / input_df) ‚Äî everything else stays in-process, byte-identical. Genuine run errors (timeout/OOM/code) raise into the existing retry path; a plumbing failure falls back to in-process (fail-soft). Timeout via env `CODE_EXEC_SUBPROCESS_TIMEOUT_S` (default 120s).
  - Verified in-container: flag OFF vs ON give identical results; infinite-loop run ‚Üí clean raise in ~2s; a child that builds an ~80MB frame leaves the parent RSS +12MB (memory not retained). Phase 1 of the sandbox plan (upload runs); live-warehouse offload = a later phase. Not yet baked into the image ‚Äî flag-gated, so OFF = today's behavior.

## v1.152.0 ‚Äî Fix "An error occurred" after a perfect result  (2026-07-07)
- Asking the agent to summarize/analyze a file sometimes showed a full, correct result and then a red **"An error occurred"** ‚Äî the turn was marked failed even though the answer was right. Fixed: a run that succeeds is now reported as a success.
  - BE `ai/code_execution/code_execution.py`: the `done` payload of `generate_and_execute_stream_v2` (and its v1 sibling) emitted the accumulated per-retry corrective feedback (`code_and_error_messages`) as `errors` **even on success**. When the coder's first attempt returned `None`/empty (very common for a print-only inspection) it self-heals and the retry returns a real DataFrame ‚Äî but the stale attempt-1 message stayed in `errors`, so `inspect_data`/`create_data` (which treat any non-empty `errors` as a failed turn) flagged the whole turn failed. Now `errors: [] if executed_successfully else code_and_error_messages` ‚Äî a successful run reports no errors; genuine end-to-end failures still surface the full retry history. Verified: gen returns None‚Üíretry‚Üídf ‚áí `errors` empty, turn succeeds. Hit most on ad-hoc chat file uploads (no Data Agent) where inspection runs a print-heavy report then `return df`.

## v1.151.0 ‚Äî Upload PDFs, Word & slides too (not just spreadsheets)  (2026-07-07)
- The single-file **Upload** picker no longer greys out PDF, Word and PowerPoint ‚Äî pick a `.pdf`, `.docx` or `.pptx` and it's accepted. Spreadsheets/CSVs still become a Data Agent; docs go to the Inbox and are routed to Knowledge when you press Train.
- Note: the mixed-folder upload (spreadsheets + docs together) already works on the latest build ‚Äî if a deployed site still drops non-spreadsheets from a folder, it's running an older build; this upgrade brings both paths current.
  - FE `components/data/UploadSpreadsheetModal.vue`: single-file `<input accept>` widened `.xlsx,.xls,.csv` ‚Üí `+.tsv,.txt,.pdf,.docx,.doc,.pptx,.md`; new `routeSingle(f)` sends a lone doc through `batchUpload([f])` (the existing type-split: data‚Üí`/data_sources/from-file`, doc‚Üí`/studios/{id}/smart-upload/inbox`) instead of the tabular `chooseFile`‚Üí`validate` reject path; `ALLOWED_EXT` += `tsv,txt` (matches the backend from-file ext gate) so lone `.txt/.tsv` pass; header/dropzone/validate copy updated. Folder input + multi-file batch were already doc-capable. Doc‚ÜíInbox needs `HYBRID_SMART_UPLOAD` (already ON org b2bec83d) + `HYBRID_DOC_KNOWLEDGE` (default ON). No backend change.

## v1.150.0 ‚Äî Everyone can upload to their own space (uploads unblocked)  (2026-07-07)
- **Any team member can now upload a file** (Excel/CSV) and get their own private Data Agent ‚Äî the file lands in their own space only, no admin needed. Previously only org admins could, so most users hit "Permission denied".
- **Super admins can upload too.** A global super admin who wasn't also given an org admin role used to be blocked from uploading (and other admin actions) inside an organization ‚Äî that gap is closed.
  - BE `core/permission_resolver.py`: `_resolve_permissions_inner` now short-circuits for a **global superuser** (`users.is_superuser`) ‚Üí grants `full_admin_access` in the resolved org permissions. Roots the fix: `is_superuser` is a GLOBAL flag, separate from the org-level `full_admin_access` role, and this fork's resolver builds org perms only from RoleAssignment/Membership (no dual-read fallback) ‚Üí a superuser with no org admin role got empty org perms ‚Üí every `requires_permission()` gate returned 403. Retroactive ‚Äî no DB change, works the moment the image ships.
  - BE `routes/data_source_from_file.py`: the `POST /data_sources/from-file` gate widened from `create_data_source` to ANY-of `['create_data_source', 'manage_files']`. `manage_files` is a baseline member permission (already seeded on every existing member role ‚Üí retroactive, no migration/backfill), and this route always forces `owner_user_id=current_user.id` + `is_public=False`, so a member can only ever create in their OWN private space. The broader `create_data_source`-only gate stays on the git / warehouse-connector / demo routes.

## v1.149.0 ‚Äî The agent can wait for your data, then pick back up  (2026-07-07)
- When the right next step is to **let time pass and retry** ‚Äî a data refresh still running, a rate limit, "try again in 30 minutes" ‚Äî the agent now **pauses and auto-resumes** instead of failing or asking you. A live countdown pill shows when it'll continue; cancel anytime.
- Wired to our Power BI reality: a 429 rate-limit or a snapshot that's still pulling is exactly when it waits. (upstream #554)
  - BE NEW `ai/tools/schemas/wait.py` (WaitInput/WaitOutput, 1‚Äì1440 min bounds) + `ai/tools/implementations/wait.py` (WaitTool, category=action, auto-registered; ends the turn via the same terminal observation path as clarify ‚Äî `analysis_complete=True` + `final_answer`). NEW `services/wait_service.py`: arms a one-shot APScheduler `date` job on the shared scheduler (`app.core.scheduler`), module-level `run_wait_wake` callable (survives SQLAlchemyJobStore serialization), cross-worker `claim_scheduled_run` dedup; on fire creates a fresh completion on the report with the pause `reason` as the prompt (full history reloads). `cancel_wait` removes the pending job.
  - BE `completion_service.cancel_wait` (initiator/owner guard, reads `job_id` from the tool execution's `result_json`, flips status ‚Üí cancelled, idempotent) + route `POST /api/completions/{cid}/tool_executions/{teid}/cancel_wait`. Planner (`prompt_builder_v3`) gains one guidance line routing pause-and-retry ‚Üí `wait`, recurring ‚Üí `create_scheduled_task`.
  - FE NEW `components/tools/WaitTool.vue`: countdown pill (live tick to `wake_at`, clock ‚Üí spinner on elapsed ‚Üí "Resuming‚Ä¶"), X to cancel (optimistic), shows the resume instruction. Wired into `getToolComponent` (`case 'wait'`) in `reports/[id]/index.vue` (explicit import). English strings inline (English-only deploys).
  - One-shot + ephemeral: no ScheduledPrompt row, self-deletes after firing once. Distinct from create_scheduled_task (recurring).

## v1.148.0 ‚Äî Dashboard "Refresh" actually refreshes (and tells you the truth)  (2026-07-07)
- **Refreshing a dashboard now re-runs its data** instead of silently doing nothing ‚Äî artifact dashboards used to show a green "refreshed" toast while staying blank.
- The refresh toast now reports the real outcome: "N of M queries refreshed" (green all-ok, orange partial, red failed, "nothing to refresh" when there's nothing to run).
- **Shared dashboards no longer go blank** after 14 days ‚Äî the data-retention cleanup now skips any report shared in any mode. (upstream #556)
  - BE `report_service.rerun_report_steps`: resolves visualization ids from the artifact being viewed (`?artifact_id=`) or the report's latest non-deleted artifact (`artifact.content['visualization_ids']`) and re-executes each query's DEFAULT step ‚Äî the path artifact dashboards actually render (they have no dashboard-layout blocks, which is why rerun was a no-op). Dashboard-layout blocks still contribute; ids deduped; unrunnable queries counted as failed. Falls back to the legacy published-widget path only when zero viz ids resolve. Thumbnail regen + subscriber notify now gated on `steps_succeeded > 0`.
  - BE returns new `ReportRerunResultSchema {message, steps_total, steps_succeeded, steps_failed, last_run_at}`; route `POST /reports/{id}/rerun` gains `?artifact_id=` + this response model (was `ReportSchema`). Scheduled-rerun caller ignores the return ‚Üí unaffected.
  - BE `maintenance_service.purge_step_payloads_for_organization`: purge SQL now also excludes reports with `artifact_visibility`/`conversation_visibility != 'none'` (the visibility source of truth), on top of the legacy `conversation_share_enabled`/`status='published'` guards.
  - FE `components/dashboard/ArtifactFrame.vue`: refresh sends `?artifact_id=`, reads the outcome, and shows honest green/orange/red toasts with "N of M queries refreshed"; clears the loading overlay in `finally`.

## v1.147.0 ‚Äî Dashboards that reflow + prompts you're allowed to see  (2026-07-06)
- **Generated dashboards now reflow cleanly** from the narrow chat side-panel to full screen ‚Äî no clipped labels, no sideways scroll. (upstream #545)
- **Saved prompts are now private to the right people** ‚Äî you only see prompts for agents you're a member of; your own and global prompts always show. Closes a gap where every member could see every prompt.
  - #545 (BE, prompt): `create_artifact.py::_build_page_prompt` gains an always-on **RESPONSIVE LAYOUT (REQUIRED)** section (fluid container, mobile-first KPI grid `grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4`, chart grids `grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2`, `overflow-x-auto` wide tables, `flex-wrap` filters, ~380px sanity check) + the closing one-word "Responsive." upgraded to a concrete rule. Explainability block untouched.
  - #555 (BE, security): new flag **`HYBRID_PROMPT_SCOPE`** (3-place, Governance, default **ON**). `prompt_service.get_prompts` + new `get_prompt_visible` filter agent-scoped prompts to explicit membership via `get_member_data_source_ids` (public agents count), private‚Üíowner-only, global‚Üíall, owner always sees own; GET `/prompts/{id}` uses `get_prompt_visible`. Our fork's `get_prompts` previously returned ALL org prompts unfiltered ‚Üí the leak. Write/manage authority unchanged (routes keep the admin bypass). Flag OFF = legacy. Fail-soft.
  - Deferred from this wave: **#550 org row-limit on refresh** ‚Äî our `format_df_for_widget` doesn't read `limit_row_count` at all, so it's a new feature (org-setting + read logic + FE toggle), not a thread-through fix. Own phase.

## v1.146.0 ‚Äî Production runs with debug OFF by default  (2026-07-06)
- Any deploy that sets `ENVIRONMENT=production` (all the shipped compose stacks ‚Äî build, nginx, NPM) now runs with debug mode **off** by default. No env change needed on the server.
  - `app/settings/production.py`: `Production` now sets `DEBUG = False` (was inheriting the base `True` from `config.py`). `development.py` still sets `DEBUG = True`, so the dev lane is unchanged. Still overridable via the `DEBUG` env var for a one-off prod investigation. Fixes the `debug_mode: TRUE` seen in a production deploy log.

## v1.145.0 ‚Äî Train your Data Agent from the header + watch it learn, live  (2026-07-06)
- New **Train** button and **Auto-train** toggle in the Data Agent header ‚Äî train on demand or let it train itself.
- Auto-train is ON by default: when a connection finishes syncing, the agent trains itself automatically.
- A **Training process** flow now sits on the agent Overview ‚Äî 9 stages (discover ‚Üí introspect ‚Üí profile ‚Üí values ‚Üí meanings ‚Üí metrics ‚Üí queries ‚Üí rules ‚Üí ready) light up as it learns, with a live log terminal and a "what got learned" summary (tables, definitions, metrics, values, rules).

Endpoints `GET/PUT /data_sources/{id}/auto-train` + `POST /data_sources/{id}/train` (busy-guarded). `connector_sync.log_step` gained `stage`; `get_run` returns `stages{}` + `learned{}` derived from the run log.

## v1.143.0 ‚Äî Power BI model introspection: the agent now knows your measures + relationships (kills DAX errors)  (2026-07-06)
- **‚òÖ The biggest Power BI DAX-error fix.** The agent used to write DAX from scratch (inventing `COUNTROWS(FILTER(...))` etc.) because it only knew table + column names ‚Äî not the model's measures or relationships. The Power BI client already had the code to pull them (`fetch_model_metadata` ‚Üí `EVALUATE INFO.VIEW.MEASURES()` / `INFO.VIEW.RELATIONSHIPS()`, `set_model_meta`, and `_model_meta_prompt` already wired into `system_prompt()`) ‚Äî but `fetch_model_metadata`/`set_model_meta` were **never called anywhere** (dead code). Wired both call sites, flag-gated `HYBRID_BI_MODEL_INTROSPECT` (default OFF), fail-soft per dataset.
  - **At sync** (`per_user_connector.sync_clone_bg`): collect the distinct `datasetId`s from `datasource_tables.metadata_json['powerbi']`, call `fetch_model_metadata` (offloaded via `asyncio.to_thread`), and persist the result to **`Connection.config['pbi_model_meta']`** (NOTE: `data_sources` has no `config` column ‚Äî model config lives on `Connection`; persisting to a DataSource attr would silently not save).
  - **At client build** (`data_source_service.construct_clients`): reload `pbi_model_meta` from the connection config and `set_model_meta(...)` on the freshly built PBI client (before the BI-snapshot router), so every `system_prompt()` carries the real measures + join graph.
  - **Verified LIVE on org b2bec83d PBI `325cee90`:** `INFO.VIEW` is NOT blocked (unlike the old `INFO.TABLES`) ‚Äî sync pulled 17 measures + 18 relationships; `construct_clients` installed 65 measures + 39 relationships (aggregated across datasets). A live query "on-risk projects count and task progress" generated DAX referencing the model's OWN measures ‚Äî `[On Risk Projects Count]`, `[Task Progress %]`, `[Total Tasks]` ‚Äî status success, **0 DAX errors**. Connector-agnostic (Fabric inherits via `PowerBIUserClient`).

## v1.142.0 ‚Äî Phase 4 (Julius-quality polish) + live query-learning fix + Power BI live-DAX fix  (2026-07-06)
- **Power BI sync crash fixed + switched to live-DAX by default.** A redundant local `import selectinload` inside the v1.140 BI-snapshot block (`per_user_connector.sync_clone_bg`) shadowed the module-level import ‚Üí `UnboundLocalError: selectinload` ‚Üí sync hard-failed whenever `BI_SNAPSHOT` was on. Removed the local import (module-level already provides it). Separately, **`BI_SNAPSHOT` is the wrong model for live BI**: it copies every row to a local DuckDB and forces the agent to write SQL against the snapshot while it (correctly) writes DAX ‚Üí "rewrite as SQL" errors. Turned `HYBRID_BI_SNAPSHOT` off; Power BI now runs **live DAX** grounded by the learned schema/column metadata. Verified live: `EVALUATE ROW(...)` returned a real answer, zero snapshot errors.
- **‚òÖ Live query-learning was wired to DEAD code ‚Äî fixed.** The `capture_live_run` hook (persist a working query to the library, record failed‚Üífixed, promote repeat successes to golden) lived ONLY in the unused `mcp/create_data.py` copy ‚Äî the LIVE tool (`implementations/create_data.py`) never captured anything, so the query library only ever grew from one-time training and `agent`-usage never improved the agent. Ported the hook into the live tool (fresh isolated session, fail-soft, connector-agnostic ‚Äî captures DAX or SQL). Verified: a live query now adds a `learned: ‚Ä¶` library row (source=chat, tags=[learned,win]); a re-ask UPSERTs the same row and, on a genuine cache-miss re-run, promotes toward golden (`GOLDEN_QUERIES` threshold 2). `HYBRID_QUERY_LEARNING` + `HYBRID_GOLDEN_QUERIES` both default on.
- **Phase 4 ‚Äî six Julius-quality features, all flag-gated OFF (byte-identical until enabled).**
  - **Smart viz picker** (`HYBRID_SMART_VIZ`) ‚Äî deterministic chart-type correction on top of the LLM pick using the existing data profile (cardinality/dtype): pie>8 cats‚Üíbar, time+numeric‚Üíline, two numerics‚Üíscatter, >50 cats‚Üítable. `create_data.py::_smart_viz_override`.
  - **Result auto-format** (`HYBRID_AUTO_FORMAT`) ‚Äî per-column display format (thousands/currency/%/date) derived from dtype+name at serialize time (`code_execution.py`), rendered as a valueFormatter (`RenderTable.vue`); raw values unchanged.
  - **Brand chart palette** (`HYBRID_BRAND_PALETTE`) ‚Äî a `brand` theme (accent #C2541E-led) becomes the default chart palette; per-report overrides still win (`themes/index.ts` + `useDashboardTheme.ts`).
  - **Parameterized report templates** (`HYBRID_PARAM_TEMPLATES`) ‚Äî saved prompts with `{{name}}` params gain a fill-in UI + a substitution/run engine that creates a report from the filled template (`prompt_run.py`, `POST /prompts/{id}/instantiate`, `prompts/index.vue`).
  - **Regenerate starters** (`HYBRID_STARTER_REFRESH`) ‚Äî a Refresh button re-runs the schema-grounded starter generator on demand (`POST /data_sources/{id}/regenerate-starters`, `agents/[id]/index.vue`); user-click only, silent in-place update (respects the blink-loop rule).
  - **Per-result interpretation** (`HYBRID_RESULT_NARRATIVE`) ‚Äî a short inline narrative per result reusing `compute_insights` (`create_data.py::_build_result_narrative`).

## v1.141.0 ‚Äî Speed Phase 3 (planner collapse ¬∑ warehouse result cache ¬∑ fast codegen) + agent-page blink fix  (2026-07-06)
- **Phase 3 of the speed plan ‚Äî three independent latency cuts, all flag-gated OFF (byte-identical until enabled).**
  - **Planner collapse** (`HYBRID_FAST_LANE + HYBRID_PLANNER_COLLAPSE`) ‚Äî when the schema + column metadata are already cached, the planner skips redundant "research the schema" steps and goes straight to codegen. Pure decision helper `app/services/speed/planner_collapse.py::plan_collapse_directive` (returns a directive + collapsed-step count, or `("",0)` when the cache signal is absent); wired into `agent_v2.py` after the FOLLOWUP_FASTPATH block, try/except fail-soft.
  - **Warehouse result cache** (`HYBRID_FAST_LANE + HYBRID_WAREHOUSE_CACHE`) ‚Äî repeat identical SQL against a warehouse-lane source returns from an in-process TTL cache (300s, 256-entry FIFO) instead of re-hitting the warehouse. `app/services/speed/result_cache.py` (key = `sha256(ds_id + normalized_sql)`, whitespace+case normalized); read-through/write-through wired into `QueryCapturingClientWrapper.execute_query` (`code_execution.py`), lane classified from the client class name, only WAREHOUSE lane eligible. Invalidated on data-source refresh (`data_source_service.py`, clear-all ‚Äî cache keyed by client name not UUID). Distinct from the pre-existing `HYBRID_RESULT_CACHE` (Learning/Redis question cache).
  - **Fast codegen** (`HYBRID_FAST_LANE + HYBRID_FAST_CODEGEN`) ‚Äî the Coder step reuses the org's small model (gemini-3.1-flash-lite) instead of the full planning model; planning/reflect untouched. `auto_model.py::codegen_model` (no hardcoded string ‚Äî resolves org small model ‚Üí `pick_model_for_tier("fast")` ‚Üí default), applied at the `create_data.py` Coder site, fail-soft.
- **Agent-page "blinking skeleton" infinite loop ‚Äî FIXED.** The `/agents/[id]` Overview page pulsed grey skeletons forever: `AgentSyncLog` emits `'done'` on every mount ‚Üí `onSyncPhase('done')` ran a NON-silent integration refetch ‚Üí toggled the layout loading flag ‚Üí `v-if/v-else` unmounted+remounted the emitting child ‚Üí it re-emitted ‚Üí ‚àû (measured ~408ms cadence, all 200-OK). Fix (`pages/agents/[id]/index.vue::onSyncPhase`): silent refetch (`injectedFetchIntegration(true)`, never touches the gating flag) + a `_syncDoneHandled` once-guard reset on any non-done phase.

## v1.140.0 ‚Äî Power BI Fast Lane: query the local snapshot (ms), not live DAX (still OFF)  (2026-07-06)
- **Phase 2 of the speed plan ‚Äî the BI query router is wired + proven.** When enabled, a Power BI / Fabric agent queries a local DuckDB snapshot of its tables with SQL (~9ms) instead of live DAX over HTTP (~seconds, throttled). Flag-gated `HYBRID_FAST_LANE + HYBRID_BI_SNAPSHOT` (default OFF) ‚Üí byte-identical until turned on; a per-agent Live mode (`data_source.config['bi_mode']='live'`) bypasses to the source.
  - `SnapshotClient` (`app/services/speed/snapshot_client.py`) ‚Äî a data-source client that speaks SQL over the DuckDB snapshot (rejects DAX, returns `List[Table]` schema, SQL-not-DAX code-gen prompt). `construct_clients` gained a gated ROUTER: for a BI-lane source with a fresh snapshot (and not Live/`prefer_live`), it swaps the live client for a `SnapshotClient`, AFTER the security access guard. New `prefer_live` kwarg lets the sync path pull from the source without self-routing. `_bi_live_mode()` reads the per-agent toggle.
  - Snapshot-on-sync: `per_user_connector.sync_clone_bg` now snapshots a BI source's tables after learn (gated, fail-soft), building per-table SPECS from `datasource_tables.metadata_json['powerbi']`.
  - ‚òÖ Root-cause fix of the pull: the BI client's offline table-index was EMPTY on this multi-dataset connector ‚Üí name‚Üídataset resolution returned (None,None) ‚Üí the client brute-probed generic names (sales/orders/‚Ä¶) and every pull failed. Fix (`bi_snapshot.py`): pass the exact `datasetId`/`workspaceId` per table EXPLICITLY (they're already in each table's metadata) ‚Üí `execute_query(dax, dataset_id=‚Ä¶, workspace_id=‚Ä¶)`, no lookup, no guess; skip `queryable=false` / empty datasets. Verified LIVE: `EDA_Toey/CityRewards_Transactions` ‚Üí 200 rows to DuckDB (no brute probe), then `SELECT COUNT(*)` in **9ms** vs live DAX seconds.
  - No migration. Backups `backend/.backups/1783324144_speedplan_phase2/`. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-v1140`. NEXT (Phase 3): planner collapse ¬∑ warehouse pushdown ¬∑ fast codegen model; (Phase 4) Julius quality (smart viz, notebooks, data-driven starters).

## v1.138.0 ‚Äî "Execution error: 'powerbi'" killed permanently (all connectors)  (2026-07-06)
- **The agent can no longer fail by guessing the wrong data-client name.** Querying Power BI (and any connector) sometimes died on the first try with "Execution error: 'powerbi'" ‚Äî a Python KeyError because the generated code wrote `db_clients['powerbi']` while the real key is the data-source name ("Power BI (User Sign-in)"). Now any reasonable key resolves to the right client, so the first attempt succeeds instead of burning a recovery turn.
  - ROOT: `data_source_service.construct_clients` keys `db_clients` by `"{ds_name}:{conn_name}"` + a bare `"{ds_name}"` alias ‚Äî never a connector-type literal. Client docstring examples hardcoded `db_clients['powerbi']` / `db_clients['sisense']`; models copied them verbatim ‚Üí `KeyError`.
  - Three layers (connector-agnostic, additive, exact-key path byte-identical): (1) **`ClientResolver(dict)`** in `ai/code_execution/code_execution.py` wraps `db_clients` at the `execute_code`/`execute_and_update_step` chokepoint ‚Äî resolves exact ‚Üí normalized (case/space/`:conn`-stripped) ‚Üí type-alias derived from the client class name (`PowerBIClient`‚Üí`powerbi`/`pbi`, `MsFabricClient`‚Üí`fabric`, `SisenseClient`‚Üí`sisense`, future connectors self-alias) ‚Üí single-client fallback ‚Üí else a clear `KeyError` listing valid keys. Every tool (create_data, inspect_data, MCP, skills) + every future connector inherits it. (2) `ai/tools/implementations/create_data.py` injects an "AVAILABLE DATA CLIENTS" block listing the real keys into the code-gen prompt (shortest/bare key per client, fail-soft). (3) `powerbi_client.py` + `sisense_client.py` examples neutralized to `db_clients[<your data source name>]` + a "don't use a connector-type name" note. Verified against the real `PowerBIClient`: `['powerbi']`/`['pbi']`/real-name/single-fallback all resolve; 2-source bad key ‚Üí clear error.
  - No migration, no flag. Backup `backend/.backups/1783321168_dbclients_keyfix/`. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-v1138`.

## v1.136.0 ‚Äî One agent's instructions never leak into another ¬∑ safer cheap-model routing ¬∑ faster small model  (2026-07-06)
- **Each agent only sees its own instructions.** Fixed the bug where a Power BI agent showed CRM instructions ("You are the MM Conso CRM analyst‚Ä¶"). Instructions built by training are now bound to their own data source, so they can't bleed across agents in the same org.
- **The fast/small model is now Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite** (was Claude Haiku 4.5) ‚Äî quicker, cheaper follow-up suggestions + sense-making.
- **Auto model routing got a safety floor.** When Auto is on, a cheap model is never handed a query it will fail: Power BI/DAX and multi-table joins get at least a mid-tier model; forecasting/why/dashboard get the reasoning tier. (Auto stays OFF until you enable it ‚Äî this is groundwork.)
  - Root cause of the leak: instructions with no data-source link were treated as org-global and force-injected (`load_mode="always"`) into every agent. Fixes: (data) linked 22 orphaned MM Conso/data-quality instructions to their source + enabled `HYBRID_SCOPED_INSTRUCTIONS` for the org (unscoped ‚âÝ global); (code) `services/train/definition_instructions.py` now binds each `AgentDefinition` instruction to its OWN `data_source_id` instead of whatever source was training at the time. Verified via the real `InstructionContextBuilder.load_always_instructions` ‚Äî Power BI loads 0 CRM instructions, MM Conso keeps its 7.
  - Auto floor: `ai/knowledge/auto_model.py::capability_floor(connector_kinds, table_count, question)` folded into `choose_auto_model`'s `min_tier` (stronger-of); wired from `completion_service.py` via cheap indexed joins (connection type set + active-table count), fail-soft, gated behind `flags.AUTO_MODEL` (OFF) so byte-identical until enabled.
  - Small model: `llm_models.is_small_default` flipped to `google/gemini-3.1-flash-lite` (data-only).
  - No migration. Backups `backend/.backups/1783318496_instrscope_automodel/`. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-v1136`.

## v1.135.0 ‚Äî Chat no longer looks blank while working ¬∑ model always named ¬∑ faster follow-ups ¬∑ Power BI stays on real tables  (2026-07-06)
- **Chat shows it's working.** The thinking shimmer now stays up while the agent plans, instead of leaving a blank center. (The early task-plan block renders only in the right-panel Progress; it no longer tricks the chat into hiding the "working‚Ä¶" indicator.)
- **Follow-up suggestions feel alive + arrive faster.** The loading state is now a named row ("Suggesting follow-ups" + a fast badge + 3 shimmer chips) instead of a blank pill, and the suggestion request is trimmed to just the question + answer (+ table names) and capped to 3 short items ‚Äî noticeably quicker.

- **Power BI answers stay grounded on your real tables.** Any model (including cheaper ones) is now given the exact dataset table names + a hard rule ‚Äî use only those names, reference columns as 'Table'[Column], never invent generic Table/Data/Measures/Dimension, no id columns. Kills the "Cannot find table 'Dimension'" / "Execution error: 'id'" DAX failures.

Power BI grounding: `powerbi_client.py::_grounding_rules_prompt`/`_real_table_names` (from cached offline `_table_index`) inserted into `system_prompt()`; `create_data.py` appends a PBI HARD-RULE block guarded on an `isinstance(PowerBIClient)` present in `ds_clients`. Additive, fail-soft, PBI-only, no execution-logic change.

## v1.134.1 ‚Äî Fix: picked agent now shows immediately (kill the double-write race)  (2026-07-06)
- **Follow-up to v1.134.0.** The binding persisted correctly to the DB, but the UI could still show the old agent (e.g. "picked Power BI, Working Folder still MM Conso"). Cause: `reports/[id]/index.vue::onAgentPickerChange` was a SECOND writer ‚Äî it PUT `data_sources` (without `studio_id`) and then `await loadReport()`, which **raced** `setReportBinding`'s commit: the refetch read while `studio_id` was still the old studio, so the effective-sources resolver returned the stale studio member and reverted the UI.
  - Fix: `onAgentPickerChange` no longer writes and no longer refetches. `DataSourceSelector.setReportBinding` is the single authoritative writer; the handler just reflects the pick locally (`currentAgents`, `report.data_sources`) + recomputes grounding ‚Äî instant, no round-trip, no race. A real reload reads the correct effective binding.
  - Removed the now-orphaned `_pickerToast`.
  - No migration, no flag. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-racefix`.

## v1.134.0 ‚Äî One binding, one truth: the agent-switch bug class, fixed permanently  (2026-07-06)
- **The report always uses the agent you picked ‚Äî and it never drifts back.** Root-cause fix for the whole "shows Power BI but queries MM Conso / can't switch off a Studio / picks revert" family. Switching between a Data Agent, an Agent Studio, or Auto now changes the report for real and sticks.
  - **One atomic write path.** `DataSourceSelector.setReportBinding()` is now the ONLY writer ‚Äî every pick PUTs `studio_id` (a real id OR explicit `null`) **and** `data_sources` together. Auto‚Üí`null`,`[]` ¬∑ Studio‚Üí`id`,members ¬∑ Data Agent‚Üí`null`,`[agent]`. So `studio_id` can finally be *cleared* (the bug: switching off a Studio never unset it ‚Üí stayed pinned to the studio's source).
  - **Backend is the single source of truth.** `GET /reports/{id}` returns *effective* `data_sources`: if `studio_id` is set it resolves the studio's member agents server-side, so the Working Folder + grounding can never show a different agent than the report actually queries. Existing studio-bound reports auto-heal on read.
  - **`update_report` honors an explicit `studio_id: null`** (exclude_unset) and replaces associations idempotently ‚Äî clearing a studio + setting new sources land in one transaction.
  - **One report per create.** Fixed the double-create: `createReport` was POSTing both `studio_id` and `data_sources`, so the backend made two reports. Now it sends ONE binding field + an in-flight guard.
  - Preserved: seed-once/pick-wins picker, `_lastPickerIds` dedupe, `loadReport` after a genuine pick, `emitDsIfChanged`.
  - No migration, no flag. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-bindingperm`.

## v1.133.0 ‚Äî Agent picker works for all three: Data Agent, Studio, Auto  (2026-07-06)
- **Switching agent now actually switches.** Picking a Data Agent, an Agent Studio, or Auto changes what the report uses ‚Äî the Working Folder and grounding follow your pick, and it sticks on reload. Previously a pick could snap back to the old agent, and picking a Studio changed nothing visible.
  - Fixes the v1.132 over-pin: the picker seeded from the report's binding on *every* tick, reverting live picks. Now it seeds **once per report** (`_seededReportKey`) and never overrides after you pick (`_userPicked`), set in all three channels.
  - **Studio picks now re-scope the report.** `selectStudio` resolves the studio's member data agents via `GET /studios/{id}/sources`, sets `data_sources` = members **plus** `studio_id`, and persists ‚Äî so the Working Folder + "Grounded on" strip (which read `data_sources`) follow the Studio, matching the backend which already scopes by `studio_id`. Fail-soft if the fetch is empty.
  - **Data Agent + Auto** paths unchanged in behavior but no longer reverted.
  - `reports/[id]/index.vue`: one `loadReport()` after a *genuine* pick (behind the `_lastPickerIds` dedupe ‚Üí no fetch loop) so the page view refreshes to the server's effective binding.
  - No migration, no flag. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-pickerall`.

## v1.132.0 ‚Äî Right data agent, every time: no more wrong-source pinning  (2026-07-06)
- **The report now uses the agent you actually picked.** Fixed the bug where a report showed "Power BI" up top but silently queried the MM Conso file. The agent picker on an open report now reflects that report's own bound data ‚Äî honest, not a stale global pick.
- **One agent selector, not two.** Removed the redundant top-nav agent pill on report pages (the composer already has the picker). It still appears on Data Agents / Workspace / Studios, where it's the only picker.
- **No more page stuck on the loading skeleton.** The report page no longer re-hydrates in a loop.

Kills the 73√ó re-hydrate storm AND the duplicate/overwritten report‚Üîsource bindings it caused.
  - P2 `components/nav/TopNav.vue`: `<AgentSelector v-if="!isReportPage">` ‚Äî hide the top pill on report routes.

  - No migration, no flag. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-agentpin`.

## v1.130.0 ‚Äî No raw JSON in chat: plans render as a checklist  (2026-07-06)
- **The agent never shows you raw code again.** When it planned its work, a technical `{"tasks":[...]}` blob could leak into the "Thought process" panel and the right-hand Answer card. Now the plan always renders as a clean **Plan checklist** (done / running / pending), and when the agent needs to ask you something you see a plain-English question ‚Äî never JSON.
  - FE `blockPlanTasks()` (`pages/reports/[id]/index.vue`) normalizes typographic/smart quotes before `JSON.parse`, so the checklist card renders even when a model emits curly quotes (was falling back to a raw dump).
  - FE `answerOf()` (`components/report/OutputsFeed.vue`) now skips `source_type='plan'` blocks and any `{"tasks":‚Ä¶}` payload, so an internal plan can never be surfaced as the Answer.
  - BE root fix: planner prompt (`agents/planner/prompt_builder_v3.py`) gains a hard rule ‚Äî never output the task-plan/JSON as reply text; ask only via the `clarify` tool. `agent_v2.py` also blanks a leaked plan-JSON `final_answer` on the clarify-action path. Fixes it for every model (bug seen on Claude Haiku 4.5), not just the FE symptom.
  - No migration, no flag. Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-planjson-fix`.

## v1.129.0 ‚Äî No more blank wait, truthful activity, faster follow-ups  (2026-07-06)
- **No more blank chat while it thinks.** The moment you send a question, the chat now shows a **shimmer "reading your data‚Ä¶" skeleton** (the same polished shimmer as the dashboard build) instead of a faint half-rendered line + a lone blinking cursor. It swaps to the real answer the instant the first words arrive.
- **The activity panel tells the truth.** The right rail used to say **"Idle ¬∑ 0/5"** while the agent was actually working; it now says **"Starting‚Ä¶"** with a live pulse the moment you send, and the plan steps gently shimmer until the first step reports.
- **Follow-up questions are faster.** When a report already looked up its tables earlier in the chat, follow-ups **skip the redundant "let me read the instructions first" step** and go straight to the answer ‚Äî cutting a full extra thinking cycle off each follow-up.
- **"No tables" flag on empty sources.** In Working Folders, a connected source that contributes **0 tables** (e.g. a Power BI sign-in with nothing usable) now shows a muted **"no tables"** badge, so it's clear why an answer might ignore it. The source stays visible.
  - FE (`frontend/pages/reports/[id]/index.vue`): new `showChatThinkingSkeleton(message)` (run active + turn has no visible content/plan/reasoning/tool yet) renders an inline shimmer card (local `.cai-sk-*` classes replicating DashboardSkeleton's warm-clay gradient ‚Äî that component renders a whole dashboard grid, wrong shape for a chat turn; `prefers-reduced-motion` guarded); `stream-caret` `v-if` gains `&& !showChatThinkingSkeleton(m)` (no orphan caret in the empty window). ACTIVITY: `activityNowLabel` = `activityNow || (runActive ? 'Starting‚Ä¶' : 'Idle')` on both NOW banners + pulse-on-runActive; `plansWarming` (`runActive && activityDoneCount===0`) shimmers pending plan badges + a 3-row shimmer for the empty step list. Working Folders: `loadDsTableCounts()` fetches `/data_sources/active?include_unconnected=true` ‚Üí `id‚Üítable_count` (the report GET's `DataSourceReportSchema.connections[].table_count` is a default 0 and unreliable), `coworkDsEmpty(ds)` true only on a confirmed 0 (never inferred) ‚Üí muted badge.
  - BE follow-up fast path (flag `HYBRID_FOLLOWUP_FASTPATH`, 3-place, default OFF, **ON for org `b2bec83d` via `hybrid_overrides`**): `backend/app/ai/agent_v2.py` `main_execution` context-assembly adds one fail-soft block (before the join-graph block) ‚Äî if this report already ran `read_resources`/`describe_tables` in a prior turn (reuses the existing `ToolExecution ‚ãà AgentExecution` query pattern) and schema/resources context is present, it appends a "FOLLOW-UP FAST PATH" hint to `PlannerInput.instructions` telling the planner the schema/instructions/resources are already in context ‚Üí drop the redundant research turn. First turn unaffected. Pure prompt nudge over always-rebuilt context (no data skipped, no stale serve); `try/except pass`, byte-identical when OFF. **Why the caches don't already cover this:** the serving funnel (`_serve_from_reasoning_cache`, Tier‚ëÝ answer_cache / Tier‚ë° reasoning_cache) keys on exact question text + data-source set, so a novel follow-up legitimately never matches ‚Äî the win is skipping the re-read, not caching the answer. No migration.

## v1.128.0 ‚Äî Agent plan now shows as a clean checklist (no more raw JSON)  (2026-07-06)
- In a report's chat, the agent's up-front plan used to dump as raw code ‚Äî a wall of `{"tasks": [{"title": ‚Ä¶, "status": "pending"}‚Ä¶]}` inside the "Thought process" box ‚Äî and a cursor kept **blinking** on it even after the run finished. Now the plan renders as a tidy **checklist card**: one row per task with a status mark (‚úì done ¬∑ spinning ring while running ¬∑ hollow circle pending) and a "done / total" counter while it works. The stray blinking cursor is gone once the answer is done. Display-only ‚Äî the agent's actual planning is unchanged.
  - `frontend/pages/reports/[id]/index.vue` (single file): new `blockPlanTasks(block, msg)` helper (~L2849) tolerantly extracts `{"tasks":[‚Ä¶]}` from the thinking block's `plan_decision?.reasoning || reasoning || content` (fast `JSON.parse`, else first-`{`‚Ä¶last-`}` slice, guarded by a `"tasks"` presence check, fail-soft `[]`; tolerates `name`/bare-string tasks). Mirrors `extractPlanTasks`' title/status mapping + `activityPlan`'s status semantics (run not in-progress ‚Üí all done; running ‚Üí first-pending = running, rest pending) rather than reusing `extractPlanTasks` (which only reads `source_type==='plan'` blocks' `content`, not `reasoning`). Template (~L368‚Äì391): `v-if="blockPlanTasks(...).length"` renders the plan card, else the existing markdown render (fallback intact). Caret (~L419): the blinking `<span class="stream-caret">` (2px clay bar, `ca-blink` in `assets/css/transitions.css:69`) was gated only on `!isBlockFinalized(block)`, which stays false forever for plan-style blocks ‚Üí now also requires `m.status === 'in_progress'`. New `.plan-card`/`.plan-glyph`/`.plan-ring` styles + `@keyframes plan-spin` with a `prefers-reduced-motion` guard. FE-only, no migration.

## v1.127.0 ‚Äî New "Connector Reports" tab: who connected + their usage  (2026-07-06)
- The **Connectors** settings page now has two tabs: **Connectors** (the usual template cards ‚Äî configure Power BI / Fabric / SharePoint / OneDrive) and a new **Connector Reports** tab. Reports shows, for each connector, **every person who connected their own account** and how they're using it: their email, live/idle/error status, when they connected, when they last used it, how many tables they synced, how many questions they've asked, tokens used, and cost. Pick a connector (Power BI, Fabric, OneDrive, SharePoint) to see just that connector's people; connectors nobody has connected show a friendly empty state. Click a person to open a detail panel with their **top questions**, a **questions-per-day** mini chart, token in/out split, average response time, and their **sync history**. A time filter (7 / 30 / 90 days) scopes the usage numbers, and **Export CSV** downloads the current connector's list. Admin-only.
  - New service `backend/app/services/connector_report.py` (org-scoped, fail-soft) mirrors `console_service.py`'s `LLMUsageRecord` group-by idioms. Two admin-gated endpoints on `backend/app/routes/data_source.py` (`full_admin`/`manage_connections`, org-scoped): `GET /api/connectors/report?days=30` ‚Üí connector groups (each: `connector_key/label/type`, `template_data_source_id`, `connected_count`, `active_7d`, `questions`, `tokens`, `cost_usd`, `last_used_at`, `users[]`), always includes ALL catalog connectors (Power BI ‚Üí Fabric ‚Üí OneDrive ‚Üí SharePoint) even with zero users, unknown types append as `other:*`; `GET /api/connectors/report/{data_source_id}?days=30` ‚Üí per-user detail (`email`, `connected_at`, `last_used_at`, `tables`, `rows`, `questions`, `tokens_in/out`, `cost_usd`, `avg_latency_ms`, `errors_7d`, `top_questions[]`, `daily_questions[]` 14d, `sync_history[]`). Data map: per-user connector = cloned `DataSource` (`owner_user_id` + `template_source_id`, `is_user_template=False`); email via `User` join; last-used = `max(LLMUsageRecord.created_at)` ‚Üí `UserDataSourceCredentials.last_used_at` ‚Üí `DataSource.last_synced_at`; questions/top-questions/daily/avg-latency from `Completion` (role='user') joined through `report_data_source_association` to the clone; tokens/cost from `LLMUsageRecord` grouped `(user_id, data_source_id)`; tables from `ConnectorSyncRun.tables_total` (fallback `COUNT(DataSourceTable)`); status = error if sync error/`phase='error'`, else live if used within 7d, else idle. FE: `frontend/pages/settings/connectors.vue` wraps the existing page body in a 2-tab switch (existing content verbatim under tab 1), new `frontend/components/connectors/ConnectorsReports.vue` (totals strip, days selector, connector pills, user table, SVG-sparkline detail drawer, client-side CSV). Not tracked per step (always null in the drawer's sync-history rows): per-step latency + per-step table count. No migration.

## v1.126.1 ‚Äî Fix: LDAP "preview sync" no longer errors  (2026-07-06)
- The LDAP directory **Preview sync** (dry-run) button was broken and would error out. Fixed ‚Äî it now correctly shows how many groups/members a sync would add or change, without writing anything. Found while running a full end-to-end LDAP test suite (connect, search users/groups, look up by email + username, sign-in bind with right/wrong password, preview + full group sync) against a live directory ‚Äî all 9 checks pass; LDAP is working.
  - Root cause: `LDAPGroupSyncService.preview_sync` called `self._get_org_user_map(db, organization_id)`, a method that never existed (only `_get_all_user_map(db)` did) ‚Üí `AttributeError` ‚Üí `GET /api/enterprise/ldap/sync/preview` 500. Fix: added `_get_org_user_map` (`backend/app/ee/ldap/sync_service.py`) ‚Äî email‚Üíuser_id scoped to the org's active `Membership` rows, which is the correct set for a dry-run (preview reports changes against current org members; a full sync separately auto-provisions non-members). No migration.

## v1.126.0 ‚Äî Non-admins no longer see Manage & Settings  (2026-07-05)
- Regular (non-admin) members now see a simpler top nav: **Agent Studios, Data Agents, Workspace, and Build** only. The **Manage** and **Settings** areas are hidden for them ‚Äî only a super-admin (full admin access) sees those. Members still reach everything they own (their reports, dashboards, connectors under Data Agents, knowledge under Build); they just don't see the org-admin surfaces.
  - `frontend/composables/useAppNav.ts`: new `superAdminOnly?: boolean` on `NavGroup`, set on the `nav.manage` + `nav.settings` groups; `visibleGroups` drops any `superAdminOnly` group unless `isAdmin` (`useCan('full_admin_access')`). This closes the gap where **Manage** showed to everyone because its `connectors` item had no per-item permission gate. FE nav visibility only ‚Äî backend per-route permissions are unchanged and still enforce access.

## v1.125.1 ‚Äî Fix: clicking a report no longer bounces to a blank page  (2026-07-05)
- Opening a saved report (one with a conversation) sometimes flipped straight to an empty "untitled report". Fixed.
  - Root cause: v1.122's `onAgentPickerChange` was bound to the composer picker's `@update:selectedDataSources`, which emits the GLOBAL selection during report load ‚Äî different from the opened report's own `data_sources`. With history + `!sameSet` it ran `navigateTo('/reports/new')`. Fix: `pages/reports/[id]/index.vue` new `agentSwitchArmed` ref (armed 1.5s after the report's data_sources settle); while unarmed `onAgentPickerChange` only syncs the local header selection and never navigates/persists ‚Äî so only genuine user agent switches branch to a new report.

## v1.125.0 ‚Äî Stop saving blank "untitled report" drafts  (2026-07-05)
- The sidebar was filling with empty "untitled report" chats you never wrote in. Now only reports that actually have a conversation are saved and listed ‚Äî blank drafts are hidden, and switching agents no longer spawns a new empty one each time. Cleaned up the 22 blanks that had piled up.
  - Root cause: `/reports/new` eagerly creates a row on mount (the "lazy" comments lied), the sidebar `GET /reports` had no empty-filter, and v1.122's `isReusable` (require draft sources == picked agent) minted a fresh orphan on every agent switch. Fixes: (a) `report_service.get_reports` now excludes placeholder-title reports with 0 completions (`title NOT IN placeholders OR EXISTS(completion)`) ‚Äî still openable by id; (b) `reports/new.vue` `isReusable` relaxed to reuse the one scratch draft + new `rescopeDraft` PUTs its `data_sources` to the picked agent (keeps the v1.122 lock, kills the multiplier); (c) one-time archive of the 22 existing blanks via the DELETE API.

## v1.124.0 ‚Äî Connector Sync Hero: table-by-table progress on the agent page  (2026-07-05)
- Connecting a Power BI / Fabric agent used to drop you on a near-blank page with a thin log ("0/0 tables") for minutes with no idea what was happening. Now the agent page shows a live **Sync Hero**: a stage strip (Sign in ‚Üí Discover ‚Üí Import ‚Üí Learn ‚Üí Ready), an overall progress bar with **elapsed + estimated time left**, and each table checking off **one by one with its row count**. You can leave the page ‚Äî it keeps syncing in the background and can notify you when it's done.
- When the sync finishes it collapses to a slim "‚úì Synced ¬∑ N tables ¬∑ N rows" ribbon and the page fills with the auto-filled instruction + starters. Partial/failed syncs show which tables were skipped and let you retry ‚Äî the ones that synced are usable immediately.
  - Backend (additive, fail-soft, **bulk DB seed unchanged**): `connector_sync.log_step` gains optional `status`/`rows` keys (JSON log, no migration); `per_user_connector.sync_clone_bg` runs the bulk seed first, then emits paced per-table `syncing‚Üídone(rows)` events grounded in the real discovered catalog (`ConnectionTable.no_rows`), `inc_tables` advancing the bar. Wrapped in try/except so progress can never break the sync.
  - FE: `AgentSyncLog.vue` rebuilt into the Sync Hero (stage strip, `tableRows` grouped from `log[]` by table, ETA, notify toggle, done ribbon, retry) ‚Äî poll/emit/self-hide preserved. `pages/agents/[id]/index.vue`: `isSyncing` gates a "Learning your data‚Ä¶" skeleton, disables the report launcher, hides the redundant discovering bar, and refetches on done. Non-syncing agents unchanged.
  - Backup: git tag `pre-sync-hero-redesign` + file copies in scratchpad.

## v1.123.1 ‚Äî Fix: connector Show/Hide toggle now actually persists  (2026-07-05)
- The connector Show/Hide toggle saved but always sprang back to "shown" (and never hid the card on the Data Agents page). Fixed ‚Äî it now sticks.
  - Root cause: `GET /organization/settings` serializes `config` through a fixed Pydantic schema (`OrganizationSettingsConfig`) that whitelists keys; `connectors_hidden` wasn't declared ‚Üí stripped on every read (saved to the DB json column by PUT, dropped on read). Added `connectors_hidden: List[str] = []` to the schema so it round-trips. Backend-only, no FE change.

## v1.123.0 ‚Äî Connector Show/Hide toggle on every row + Test before save  (2026-07-05)

FE gates Save on `testResult.ok`, resets on field edit. Note: toggle PUT needs `manage_settings` (super-admin has it). ‚Äî Connector Disable/Enable label + each report stays on its own agent's data  (2026-07-05)
- The connector **Enable / Disable** button now reads properly (it was showing a raw code label). Disabling a connector hides it from the Data Agents page; enabling brings it back.
- **A report now stays locked to the agent's own data.** Before, opening a report and switching the agent in the picker changed the title to the new agent but the working folders + "Grounded on‚Ä¶" still showed the old agent's data. Now: switch agent in a fresh report ‚Üí its data follows; switch in a report that already has a conversation ‚Üí it opens a **new report** on the new agent instead of quietly re-grounding the old chat.
  - Bug 1: five `connectors.*` i18n keys were missing (`disable/enable/disabledChip/disabled/enabled`); vue-i18n returns the raw key (truthy) so the `$t()||'x'` fallback never fired. Added to `locales/en.json`.
  - Bug 2: working-folders + grounding scope to persisted `report.data_sources`, but the composer picker only mutated the live `currentAgents` ref (header) without persisting. `reports/[id]/index.vue` new `onAgentPickerChange`: history+changed ‚Üí seed `useAgent().selectAgents` + `/reports/new`; fresh ‚Üí PUT `/reports/{id}` `{data_sources}` + reload grounding. `reports/new.vue` `isReusable` now also requires the stale draft's sources match the picked agent. Backend `report_service.create_report` Data-Agent path (no `studio_id`) drops any `data_source_id` not in the org (fail-soft, all-valid = no-op). ‚Äî Teach the agent: metrics, queries & a downloadable template  (2026-07-05)
- Teach the agent now creates **Metrics, Queries and verified Q&A examples** too ‚Äî not just rules and skills. Paste "Total leads = 1,544, Logic: ‚Ä¶" and it becomes a real locked Metric; a named SQL becomes a golden Query; a Q/A becomes an Example.
- **Three ways to teach:** type one rule at a time, paste many at once, or **download a template, fill it offline, and upload it** ‚Äî the agent reads the file and proposes everything to review before saving.
- Download the template as **Markdown or Excel** (Metrics / Queries / Examples / Data rules / Skills / Instructions / Knowledge sections). A "Load template into box" helper drops a starter snippet in for quick one-off teaching.
  - Backend: `_SPAN_TYPES` + `_CLASSIFY_PROMPT` gained `METRIC`/`QUERY`/`EXAMPLE`; `apply_spans` persists to `metric_definitions` (locked/last_value when a value is given), `query_library_items` (`source=teach`, `is_golden`), `studio_examples` (pending), each fail-soft. `preview_spans` passes the sub-objects + `will_be` through so the review cards render them.
  - New `app/ai/packs/teach_template.py` (`build_template_md`/`build_template_xlsx`/`parse_upload`, openpyxl). Two routes on `studio_teach.py`: `GET /studios/{id}/teach/template?fmt=md|xlsx` (download) + `POST /studios/{id}/teach/upload` (multipart ‚Üí parse ‚Üí same classify+preview pipeline, ‚â§2MB). FE `StudioTeach.vue`: download dropdown, upload button, METRIC/QUERY/EXAMPLE badges + card enrichment. Reuses flag `TEACH_BOX`.
Bullet rules (this is the user-facing "What's new" feed):
  - **Top-level** `- ` bullets are USER-FACING ‚Äî plain language, no file paths / jargon / markdown.
    These show in the in-app "What's new" popover.
  - **Indented** `  - ` bullets are TECHNICAL detail ‚Äî file paths, flags, internals.
    Hidden from the popover; shown collapsed on the full /changelog page only.
Every shipped feature bumps `VERSION_HYBRID` and adds an entry here.

## v1.120.0 ‚Äî Color-coded robot log + wider terminal, enable/disable connectors, only show configured ones  (2026-07-05)
- The robot terminal is now **wider** and **color-coded**: stages read clay, successes green, errors red, held/skipped amber, model names violet, ids/tables dim grey, and numbers pop in cyan ‚Äî so you can scan a run at a glance instead of a wall of one color.
- **Connectors can be turned on/off.** In Settings ‚Üí Connectors, each configured connector (Fabric, Power BI) has an **Enable/Disable** toggle. A disabled connector stays configured but disappears from the Data Agents page and can't be signed into.
- **The Data Agents page now shows only connectors that are actually set up.** Unconfigured connectors are hidden from members (admins still see them to set up), and a connector only shows "‚úì Connected" when its sign-in actually has data ‚Äî so the old "Microsoft Fabric: Needs setup AND Connected" contradiction (a leftover empty sign-in) is gone.
  - `components/studio/StudioRobotDock.vue`: dock `width: min(92vw, 620px)`; per-line `lineClass` (error>held>success>stage>model>default) + escape-first `renderMsg` inline highlights (`hl-num` cyan for counts, `hl-id` dim mono for org/table ids); `.srd-msg.lvl-*` CSS. Day-breaker/single-stamp/model-while-running intact.
  - `services/per_user_connector.py::list_available_templates`: each row now returns `publish_status` + `config`; dropped the server-side disabled-skip (FE decides via `isConfigured`).
  - `pages/settings/connectors.vue`: `isDisabled`/`toggleTemplate` ‚Üí `PUT /data_sources/{id}` `{publish_status:'disabled'|'published'}`; Enable/Disable button + muted "Disabled" chip on configured rows.
  - `components/connectors/ConnectorsMsHub.vue`: `visibleCatalog` computed (`!c.live || isConfigured(c) || canManage`) so unconfigured/disabled live tiles hide from members; `readyCloneFor` (clone with `ready`/`table_count>0`) gates the "Connected" branch. Coming-soon SharePoint/OneDrive still render. (Report-footer gap: no change ‚Äî already `mt-2` under the composer.)

## v1.119.0 ‚Äî No more red ingest errors: skip the redundant DuckDB re-ingest  (2026-07-05)
- Training used to print two scary (but non-fatal) red lines on every file: `dlt_ingest failed ‚Ä¶ same database file with a different config` and `quality_gate failed ‚Ä¶ Table t_‚Ä¶ does not exist`. Root cause: the file's rows were already written and registered by the direct loader, then a second, redundant step tried to re-import the same data into a separate DuckDB file, hit DuckDB's single-writer lock, failed, and the quality check then looked for a table that step never created. Now that redundant step is skipped whenever the loader already wrote the rows ‚Äî so the errors are gone and ingest is faster.
  - `routes/data_source_from_file.py`: both ingest branches (new-source ~L676 + same-schema append ~L343) now skip the `dlt_ingest` + `quality_gate` block when the direct loader (`upload_persist`, gated `HYBRID_PERSIST_WAREHOUSE`) already persisted rows (`warehouse["tables"]` non-empty ‚Üí `_loader_persisted`/`_append_persisted`). `reconcile` (4c3) remains the real post-ingest validation. dlt still runs as a fallback when persist wrote nothing. Verified live: a CRM train now logs 0 `dlt_ingest failed` + 0 `quality_gate failed`.

## v1.118.0 ‚Äî Finished trains now read 100% (no-op steps show as "skipped")  (2026-07-05)
- The process flow used to stall at e.g. 91% after a train finished, because steps that had nothing to do (like ingest when there were 0 new inbox files, or coverage with 0 periods) stayed grey. Now, once a run completes, those no-op steps show as **skipped** (a muted ‚úì ‚Äî nothing to do), the bar reaches **100%**, and the **‚úì Agent ready** circle turns green. Steps that genuinely need attention still show as held.
  - `components/studio/StudioAutopilotV2.vue`: added `runComplete` (train log `all stages complete`/`agent ready`, or status ‚àà done/complete/ready/‚Ä¶, or `flowAllDone`) and a `_resolvedFlow` wrapper that remaps `queued ‚Üí skipped` ONLY when `runComplete` (active runs unchanged). `flowPct` now counts done+skipped+held as resolved; new `flowReady` drives the terminal/label. New `st-skipped` state (dim ‚úì) + legend entry. Rebased `flowAllDone` off raw `trainFlow` to avoid a computed cycle.

## v1.117.0 ‚Äî Full process-flow diagram + training now uses your chosen model  (2026-07-05)
- The training view is now a proper process diagram: every step is its own icon box, connected left‚Üíright by arrows, with a "router" decision that branches anything it wasn't sure about down to a "Held ¬∑ review" spot, ending in a green ‚úì "Agent ready" circle. Steps light up as they run (amber, spinning) and turn green with a tick when done. Covers all ~20 real steps and scrolls sideways.
- Fixed: training was ignoring the Training model you set in Settings ‚Üí LLM (Agent Defaults) and always used the analysis default (Claude). Now a train run uses your configured Training model ‚Äî e.g. Gemini 3.5 Flash ‚Äî as it should.
  - `components/studio/StudioAutopilotV2.vue`: replaced the 6-phase column flow with a horizontal BPMN spine (`bpmn-*`): route group ‚Üí decision diamond ("router sure?") + held-branch terminal ‚Üí all pipeline stages as inline-SVG icon boxes ‚Üí ‚úì Agent-ready terminal. Extended `FLOW_PHASES` to 22 nodes (added queries/artifacts/semantic/mine-joins/verified-goldens/docs + aliases); reused existing `trainFlow`/state derivation, `flowPct`/`flowAllDone`; running box shows amber ring+pulse (reduced-motion safe), done shows ‚úì badge. Pills + trigger buttons untouched. `overflow-x:auto` scroll, no page-level sideways scroll.
  - `ai/knowledge/train_orchestrator.py`: the main "CHOSEN train model ONCE" resolver only read `studio.config` then fell back to the org DEFAULT (analysis) model. Added the missing middle step ‚Äî `organization_settings.config['default_train_model_id']` (Agent Defaults ‚Üí Training) ‚Äî mirroring the `route_inbox` precedence: studio model ‚Üí org training default ‚Üí analysis default. Verified live: log now prints `train model: google/gemini-3.5-flash`.

## v1.116.0 ‚Äî Training now shows a live process flow, not flat chips  (2026-07-05)
- The Auto-pilot "3 ¬∑ TRAIN" card now shows the whole training pipeline as a live flow: 6 phases (Route ‚Üí Land ‚Üí Profile ‚Üí Enrich ‚Üí Learn ‚Üí Verify) connected by arrows, each with its real sub-stages. Every step lights up as it goes ‚Äî green ‚úì when done, amber ‚ü≥ while running, grey when queued, dashed when it couldn't run (honest ‚Äî e.g. coverage with 0 periods). A slim bar up top reads `running ¬∑ 62%` and flips to `‚úì agent ready ¬∑ 100%` when the agent finishes.
  - `components/studio/StudioAutopilotV2.vue`: replaced the flat `receiptStages` chip row with a `trainFlow` computed (6 phases √ó real stage nodes) + `flowPct`/`flowAllDone`. Node state derived fail-soft from live `/train/status`: reuses `receiptStages` done-flags for the 6 mapped nodes, resolves the rest from `status.detail[key]` (with aliases: profile‚Üîprofiling, deep-profile‚Üîprofile_v2, index‚Üîhybrid_index, domain-packs‚Üîpacks, etc.), running from the newest `‚ñ∏ <stage>` log marker (only while `trainingAll`), held for coverage=0. Never forces green on unknown ‚Üí 'queued'. Pills (`N in‚ÜíN placed¬∑N held`, `coverage N periods`) kept below. Scoped CSS + `flow-spin` keyframe (respects prefers-reduced-motion). No backend change.

Its log reads cleaner: one timestamp on the left of each line (the confusing second stamp on the right is gone), a full-width date divider whenever the log crosses into a new day, and the model name shows under the robot only while it's actually working (hidden when idle).

## v1.114.0 ‚Äî Uploaded files no longer show up as their own Data Agent in the pickers  (2026-07-05)
- An uploaded file (like a CSV) that belongs to an Agent Studio was wrongly appearing as its own line under "Data Agents" in the New-report picker and the top-right picker ‚Äî duplicating data that already lives inside its studio. Now the "Data Agents" group in both pickers shows only real connector agents (Power BI, Fabric, SharePoint, OneDrive), exactly like the Data Agents page. Your file still shows inside its studio (e.g. CRM) under "Agent Studios" ‚Äî you pick the studio, not the raw file.
  - Root cause: the `/agents` page filters to `connector_kind` (v1.104) but the two pickers never got that filter. `services/data_source_service.py::get_active_data_sources` also never populated `connector_kind` (always null on `/data_sources/active`) ‚Üí mirrored the derivation from `get_data_sources` (connection type ‚àà {powerbi_user, ms_fabric, sharepoint, onedrive}, else null; reuses the eager-loaded connection, no N+1). FE: `components/prompt/DataSourceSelector.vue` (`getDataSources` now `isUsable(ds) && CONNECTOR_KINDS.has(ds.connector_kind)`) + `components/AgentSelector.vue` (`dataAgents` computed adds `CONNECTOR_KINDS.has(a.connector_kind)`); both carry a self-contained `CONNECTOR_KINDS` set matching `pages/agents/index.vue`. Agent Studios group untouched. Verified live: `/data_sources/active` ‚Üí Power BI=powerbi_user, Fabric=ms_fabric, CSV=null.

Connect Fabric and you get a Fabric agent; connect Power BI and you get a Power BI agent. Each signs in on its own, so there are no surprise extra agents. Any agents you already connected stay exactly as they are.
