## v1.112.0 ‚Äî Claude-style thinking: streams step-by-step while working, collapses to a summary when done  (2026-07-05)
- The agent's thinking now reads like a clean timeline: while it works, each step appears one at a time (planning, reading the source, building the dataset, checking quality) with a calm "Working‚Ä¶" line and a live timer; the moment it finishes, the whole thing folds to a single "Worked for 14s ¬∑ ‚Ä¶" line you can click to reopen. No more busy spinner blob, and the internal task-plan JSON never shows up as the answer.
  - `components/AgentStepTimeline.vue`: replaced the `.cai-wave` weave + `Thought process ¬∑ N steps` pill with a streaming-expanded timeline (running header = slow-spin clay spark + `Working‚Ä¶` + `M:SS`; per-step clay rail with `node-run` pulse / `node-done` fill / `+N.Ns` / monospace tool box). Auto-collapse on live finish (`watch(isRunning)` ‚Üí 500ms ‚Üí `collapsed=true`), reloaded completions mount collapsed (`collapsed = status !== 'in_progress'`). Header `‚åÑ Worked for {totalSeconds}s ¬∑ {summary}`. 100% derived from the existing `steps` prop ‚Äî no hardcoded titles/tools/counts (summary counts real `kind==='tool'` steps + row counts regex'd from real `body.output`). Respects `prefers-reduced-motion`.
  - `utils/stepMap.ts`: `prettyTool` generic fallback ‚Äî any unmapped `tool_name` narrates as `Ran <Prettified Name>` (new `prettify()`), neutral wrench icon; known `TOOL_MAP` kept; `source_type==='plan'` skip intact.
  - `pages/reports/[id]/index.vue`: calmed the two inline running headers (clay spark + `Working‚Ä¶` + live `runningStageText` + elapsed, same state/logic); decision shimmer softened to `Forming the decision‚Ä¶`. Plan-JSON leak already fully guarded (`source_type !== 'plan'`), audited.
- Backup/restore point: git tag `pre-thinking-ui-1783256770`, files in `scratchpad/backup_thinking_ui_1783256770/`.

## v1.111.0 ‚Äî Repeated prompts no longer answer with an empty bubble  (2026-07-05)
- Asking the same thing twice used to return a blank reply (and skip the clarifying questions) ‚Äî now it re-runs and answers properly instead of serving a hollow cached result.
  - `ai/agent_v2.py::_serve_from_reasoning_cache` (~L1932): the serving-funnel answer cache short-circuits the whole agent loop on a cache hit, but a DEGENERATE hit (blank markdown or `row_count <= 0`) rendered as an empty assistant bubble AND skipped the clarifying-question step (repeated identical prompts served a 0-row entry ‚Äî log tell `serving-funnel answer_cache hit (0 rows, 0 LLM)`). Guard added: `if not outcome.served or not (outcome.answer_md or '').strip() or getattr(outcome,'row_count',0) <= 0: return False` ‚Üí fall through to a real run. Correctness > cache.

## v1.110.0 ‚Äî Chat tables scroll instead of shredding into letter-by-letter columns  (2026-07-05)
- Wide tables in a chat answer no longer crush every column so words break mid-letter ‚Äî the table now scrolls sideways and each column gets real width, so text wraps on spaces and stays readable.
  - `components/CompletionMessageComponent.vue` `:deep(.markdown-content) table`: markdown emits a bare `<table>` (no wrapper), so the table itself is the scroll box ‚Äî `display:block; width:max-content; max-width:100%; overflow-x:auto` (grow to content, capped at the chat column width, scroll when wider) replacing the old `w-full`. Cells gain `min-width:6rem; white-space:normal; word-break:normal; overflow-wrap:normal; vertical-align:top`; first (label) column `white-space:nowrap`. CSS-only, no template/JS change.

## v1.109.0 ‚Äî Source-lock: the answer comes ONLY from the source you picked, and empty sources refuse instead of guessing  (2026-07-05)
- Both source pickers (the top bar and the one in the chat box) now stay in sync ‚Äî pick a source in one, it's selected in the other. No more picking Power BI in one place and getting an answer from a different file.
- Every source now shows whether it has data: a green "ready" dot with the table count, a red "no data" dot, or an amber "sign in" dot.
- If you pick a source that has no synced data (e.g. an empty Fabric warehouse), the agent now refuses and tells you to sync it first ‚Äî it will NOT quietly answer from another source. A Sync button takes you straight to fix it.
  - **Mirrored pickers:** `components/prompt/DataSourceSelector.vue` now writes data-source picks into the shared `useAgent()` store (`selectAgents`) and reads top-bar picks back via a `watch(globalSelectedAgents)` (deep, landing-only guard `if (props.reportId) return` so a live report keeps its bound sources; re-synced after `getDataSources()`). One-directional per trigger + equal-set short-circuit = no feedback loop. Studio picks were already shared.
  - **Readiness contract:** `services/data_source_service.py` ‚Äî new `count_active_tables_by_source(db, ids)` (single grouped COUNT over `DataSourceTable` where `datasource_id IN ‚Ä¶ AND is_active`, no N+1) feeds `table_count`+`ready` (`= table_count>0`) onto every item from `get_data_sources` and `get_active_data_sources`; fields added to `schemas/data_source_schema.py::DataSourceListItemSchema` (default 0/False). FE `readyState(ds)` renders green/red/amber pills; helpers fail-OPEN when fields absent.
  - **Sync-gate refuse:** flag `HYBRID_SOURCE_SYNC_GATE` (default ON, `settings/hybrid_flags.py`, 3-place). `completion_service.py` ‚Äî after each AGENT_ACL gate (non-stream ~L744, stream ~L2441), if every bound `report.data_sources` has 0 active tables ‚Üí write a refusal completion ("I can't answer from **{names}** yet ‚Äî it has no synced data. I won't use another source instead. Sync it first‚Ä¶") as a `status='success'` answer (non-stream returns it; stream persists + emits a `block.upsert` SSE then returns cleanly). Proceeds normally if ANY bound source has tables. AGENT_ACL/`studio_access.py` untouched.
  - **FE gate:** `PromptBoxV2.vue` ‚Äî `selectedSourceReady` computed (true for studio/Auto/any-ready pick; false only when a specific picked source is unready) gates `canSubmit`; `submit()`+`createReport()` early-return; refuse banner above the composer with **Sync {name}** (‚Üí `/agents/{id}`) + **Switch source** (re-opens picker).
  - Verified live: `/data_sources/active` now returns Power BI `table_count=10 ready=true`, Fabric `0/false` (‚Üí will refuse), CSV `1/true`.

## v1.108.0 ‚Äî Chat no longer 403s on agents whose studio was deleted ¬∑ Fabric picks a real warehouse ¬∑ connector edit/delete  (2026-07-05)
- Chatting a data agent no longer fails with "You do not have access to this agent" after its studio was removed ‚Äî the agent keeps working on its own.
- Microsoft Fabric now syncs your real data instead of coming up empty ‚Äî it skips the throwaway staging warehouse Fabric creates automatically.
- You can now edit or remove a configured Microsoft connector from Settings ‚Üí Connectors, not just create one.
  - **403 fix:** reports can outlive a soft-deleted `Studio`, leaving a stale `report.studio_id`. The `AGENT_ACL` gate called `resolve_studio_access` (which filters `deleted_at IS NULL`) ‚Üí `None` ‚Üí 403 even for the org owner. NEW `services/studio_access.py::studio_chat_gate(db, studio_id, user)` ‚Äî raw `select(Studio)` (no `deleted_at` filter): missing/soft-deleted studio ‚Üí allow (report falls back to plain data-agent chat); `is_superuser` or `resolve_permissions`‚Üí`FULL_ADMIN` ‚Üí allow; else `resolve_studio_access is not None`. Wired into BOTH `completion_service.py` gate sites (~L554 non-stream, ~L2131 stream), replacing the direct `resolve_studio_access` check. `routes/studio_reports.py` + `routes/external_platform.py` left untouched (they gate LIVE studio ops ‚Äî correct as-is). DATA: `UPDATE reports SET studio_id=NULL WHERE studio_id IN (SELECT id FROM studios WHERE deleted_at IS NOT NULL)` cleared 4 stale rows (backup `scratchpad/stale_studio_backup_*.csv`).
  - **Fabric fix:** `services/ms_fabric_discovery.py::discover_fabric_endpoint` took the FIRST warehouse/lakehouse found ‚Üí grabbed the empty auto-generated `StagingWarehouseForDataflows_<ts>` ‚Üí `get_schemas()` returned 0 tables. Now collects ALL candidates, then picks by priority via `_is_staging()` (case-insensitive match on `StagingWarehouseForDataflows`/`ForDataflows`/`staging*`/`*_staging`): first non-staging warehouse ‚Üí first non-staging lakehouse ‚Üí first-anything fallback (honest empty). Return shape unchanged (`server_hostname`/`database`/`workspace`/`n_warehouses`); logs chosen warehouse + staging-skip count.
  - **connector edit/delete:** `pages/settings/connectors.vue::publishTemplate` now PUTs `/data_sources/{id}` when a template already exists (POST tripped the unique-name guard ‚Üí "already exists"); added `deleteTemplate` (`DELETE /data_sources/{id}`) + a Delete button + Save/Publish label toggle. `services/data_source_service.py::get_active_data_sources` now excludes `is_user_template` (matches `get_data_sources`) so the config-shell template stops appearing as a phantom "Service account" agent in the composer picker.

## v1.107.0 ‚Äî Glossary/semantic files no longer dropped when applied with a brand-new agent  (2026-07-05)
- When you upload a spreadsheet and a glossary together onto a brand-new agent, the glossary now attaches correctly instead of being silently skipped ‚Äî no matter which file you dropped first.
  - `services/smart_upload/apply.py::apply_routes`: added a `data_source_id` backfill ‚Äî the run now processes `database` dests first (stable-sorted working copy, caller's list never mutated) and tracks `effective_ds_id`, set from the newly-created source's `data_source_id`. The `semantic`/`knowledge` sinks now bind to `effective_ds_id` instead of the still-`None` outer param, so a same-batch glossary on a new agent no longer raises "semantic routing needs a target data_source_id" and gets dropped. Summary dict now echoes `data_source_id`.

## v1.106.0 ‚Äî Deleting an agent now cleans up everything  (2026-07-05)
- Removing an agent from the hub now also frees its stored data and any empty container it left behind ‚Äî nothing lingers taking up space, and an emptied studio no longer shows up with no source.
  - `data_source_service.delete_data_source`: before the child sweep, collect (schema, physical_table) from `connection_tables` joined on `datasource_tables`, guarded ‚Äî only this org's own `staging_<org>` schema, identifier-allowlisted (`^[A-Za-z0-9_]+$`), and skipped if any OTHER live data source still references the same physical table.
  - After the parent hard-delete: soft-delete now-empty studio shells (`UPDATE studios SET deleted_at=now()` when `studio_data_sources` count for that studio hits 0; multi-source studios untouched), then `DROP TABLE IF EXISTS "<schema>"."<table>" CASCADE` on the raw `loader_write_engine` via `asyncio.to_thread` (off the async greenlet). All fail-soft ‚Äî residue is inert, never a 500.
  - Brings UI agent-delete to parity with a manual org wipe (physical staging blobs dropped + studio shell hidden), closing the two gaps left by the earlier hard-delete hardening.

## v1.105.0 ‚Äî Self-healing ingest: your data is always complete (any dataset)  (2026-07-05)
- Upload the same kind of file in different sessions (e.g. one month at a time) and it now all lands in ONE agent table automatically ‚Äî no more "the agent only sees April."
- If some files fail to load, the upload now tells you loudly ("N of M files didn't land") instead of silently showing partial data, and the agent is warned not to make up the missing periods.
- New "Repair data" action (and an automatic pass at training time) detects an agent whose data got split across leftover tables and stitches it back together ‚Äî safely, for any dataset, not just months.
- Files a user uploads (and the insights generated from them) are usable by the agent immediately ‚Äî no more "12 documents stuck pending / invisible."
  - Flags flipped ON by default + 2 new (all 3-place in `hybrid_flags.py`): `HYBRID_ONE_TABLE_MERGE` ON, `HYBRID_INGEST_RECONCILE` ON (stable), new `HYBRID_INGEST_SELFHEAL` ON, new `HYBRID_AUTOEDA_AUTOAPPROVE` ON.
  - P1 cross-session merge (`routes/data_source_from_file.py` + `data_sources/clients/spreadsheet_client.py`): `_try_merge_same_schema` now matches by tolerant column-signature (`_same_template`: order/case-insensitive + bounded ¬±10% column drift), prefers the target studio's already-bound source (new optional `studio_id` on the request + `_studio_bound_ds_ids`), and `_load_frames` groups by same-template signature (not exact hash) so tolerant matches still stack into one table with a `_source_period` partition column.
  - P2 completeness gate: `HYBRID_INGEST_RECONCILE` on ‚Üí multi-file merge records each file's outcome, flips the source DEGRADED on shortfall, stamps `ingest_coverage` on the connection + tables, surfaces it in the upload response, and `tables_schema_section._render_coverage_note` injects a "DATA COVERAGE WARNING ‚Äî do NOT fabricate missing periods" into agent context. Fail-soft.
  - P3 self-heal (`services/ingest/selfheal.py` NEW): `selfheal_data_source` resolves the DS's bound staging table + column-signature, finds unclaimed same-signature orphan tables in the org schema (never steals another live agent's table), backs up, then single-transaction `INSERT‚Ä¶SELECT‚Ä¶WHERE NOT EXISTS` (idempotent on `_row_key`/`_content_hash`/full-row), updates `no_rows`, optional drop-orphans. Wired as fail-soft train Stage 0b (`train_orchestrator.py`) + `POST /api/data_sources/{id}/repair` (`?dry_run`, owner/admin) + "Repair data" button (`StudioAutopilotV2.vue`). Proven idempotent (dry-run tables_stitched=0 on the healed CRM agent; synthetic-orphan merge+dedupe verified).
  - P4 first-party auto-approve (`ai/knowledge/docs_index.py`): single choke-point `ingest_doc` gained `_resolve_ingest_status(source, approve)` ‚Äî first-party (`source='upload'` or `approve=True`) lands `approved` when `HYBRID_AUTOEDA_AUTOAPPROVE` on; learned/AI-proposed memories (separate models, never through `ingest_doc`) keep the review gate. Fail-soft ‚Üí pending.

## v1.104.0 ‚Äî No more duplicate agents: hub is connectors-only + create-agent-first  (2026-07-05)
- The Data Agents hub now shows ONLY connector agents (Power BI, Fabric, SharePoint, OneDrive). Uploading a spreadsheet no longer spawns a phantom "data agent" twin next to your Studio.
- Creating an agent is now explicit: make the agent first, then add data to it ‚Äî either upload files or connect a source. Dropping a file no longer silently creates an agent behind your back.
  - Root cause: in this fork a DataSource *is* a Data Agent, so a Studio's uploaded file (a private `spreadsheet` DataSource) was being listed on the /agents hub as a twin. The hub filter only dropped templates + others' public agents; it never excluded file/studio-backing sources.
  - Backend: new fail-soft `connector_kind` on the data-source list (`schemas/data_source_schema.py` + `services/data_source_service.py::get_data_sources`, reuses the already-eager-loaded first connection, no N+1) = the backing connection type when it's one of `powerbi_user|ms_fabric|sharepoint|onedrive`, else null. B1 audit: no upload path sets `is_public=True` (uploads stay private + studio-bound via `StudioDataSource`) ‚Äî the twin was purely the hub *listing*.
  - Frontend: `pages/agents/index.vue` `allAgents` now includes an item ONLY when `connector_kind` ‚àà the 4 (uploads/null excluded); added a single "New agent" button (header + empty state) ‚Üí `/agents/new`. `pages/agents/new/index.vue` gained an Add-data toggle (Upload files | Connect a source); the upload branch creates the agent from the file via `/files` ‚Üí `/data_sources/from-file` named from the wizard (the DataSource IS the agent), then walks the same schema‚Üícontext steps. `locales/en.json` `data.newAgent`.

## v1.99.0 ‚Äî BI uplift Phase 7: predictions by AI  (2026-07-05)
- Ask the agent to predict, and it now can ‚Äî forecast where a trend is heading, score which rows are at risk (churn, hot leads), or surface hidden patterns in your latest result.
- Each data agent's Overview now has a Forecast card ‚Äî one click projects the next few months of its main trend, with a low‚Äìhigh range and the reasoning behind it.
  - Agent-Overview forecast surface: `services/analytics/agent_forecast.py::build_agent_forecast` reuses the agent's Auto-EDA time series (`eda_profile.profile.time_series.points`, real monthly aggregate ‚Äî no re-query), LLMTime + `infer_samples(n=3)` self-consistency. `_resolve_claude_reason_model` PINS an enabled Claude model (opus>sonnet>haiku) per the "Claude reasoning" ask, else falls back to the reasoning tier ‚Äî verified resolving to `anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.6`. Route `POST /data_sources/{id}/forecast` (gated ADV_METHODS, mirrors `/kpis`). FE `components/AgentDetail.vue` Forecast card (Predict/Refresh button, history‚Üíforecast points + band + direction/confidence chips + assumptions + AI-estimate badge; gated on `edaProfile.time_series || forecast`). Transient (no DB column).
- Every prediction is clearly labelled an "AI estimate" and comes with its assumptions, a low‚Äìhigh range, and a confidence level, so you know how much to trust it.
- Predictions reason over your real numbers ‚Äî nothing is invented ‚Äî and are turned off unless your workspace enables them.
  - BI-uplift Phase 7 = LLM-as-predictor, NO local ML engine (no statsmodels/sklearn/scipy). Three flag-gated tools (`HYBRID_ADV_METHODS`, default OFF; ON org b2bec83d): `forecast_llm` (LLMTime ‚Äî serialize series‚Üíreasoning model extrapolates, `infer_samples(n=3)` self-consistency ‚Üí per-period median + min/max band + spread-based confidence), `classify_llm` (TabLLM ‚Äî serialize each row‚Üílabel+confidence+reason, ‚â§40 rows/call, snaps to allowed labels), `discover_llm` (associations/relationships/segments ‚Äî pandas computes real category shares / co-occurrence crosstab / correlations, LLM interprets; never invents a pattern absent from the counts).
  - Shared primitives `app/services/analytics/llm_predict.py`: `resolve_reason_model` (routes to Claude reasoning tier via `auto_model.pick_model_for_tier("reason",‚Ä¶)`), `infer`/`infer_samples` (off-thread sync `LLM.inference`), `extract_json`, `fetch_latest_step_df` (LoadablesResolver ‚Üí grid_to_df ‚Üí hydrate), `guess_series`/`serialize_series`. `AI_ESTIMATE` disclaimer stamped on every output.
  - Planner-catalog gate in `app/ai/registry.py` (`ADV_METHOD_TOOLS`, read at call time) hides all three when the flag is OFF so the planner never advertises a self-no-op tool. Flag added 3-place in `settings/hybrid_flags.py` (P0).

## v1.98.0 ‚Äî BI uplift Phase 3: per-agent KPI layer  (2026-07-05)
- Each agent now defines its own **key metrics** on its Overview: outcome-first KPIs (a conversion/success rate beats a raw count), each tagged **leading** or **lagging** with what it leads to, plus a target and an action to take if it goes off-track. Refreshable on demand.
  - New `services/analytics/agent_kpis.py::build_agent_kpis` (flag `HYBRID_KPI_LAYER`): reuses the agent's EDA profile (or computes one) ‚Üí LLM proposes 3-6 governed KPIs grounded on real columns only (activity counts get a suggested outcome ratio in `better`) ‚Üí persist to `data_sources.kpi_defs`. Train stage `agent_kpis` (after `auto_eda`, reuses the fresh profile), on-demand `POST /data_sources/{id}/kpis`, `kpi_defs` already on `DataSourceSchema`/service, render in `components/AgentDetail.vue` Overview ("Key metrics" with leading/lagging + outcome/activity chips). Compute-then-narrate + fail-soft. Live breach alerting on real per-period values is deferred (structure defined now). Off = no KPI section.

Requires `HYBRID_SENSE_MAKING` on (the card itself). Verified with a real LLM call on a synthetic declining series ‚Äî coherent grounded CCR + real-column-only drivers, existing headline/findings/alerts intact.

## v1.95.0 ‚Äî BI uplift: chart guardrail + per-agent Auto-EDA (foundation)  (2026-07-05)
- Two analyst-grade upgrades from the "BI learning" framework set, both flag-gated and off by default (on for this org):
  - **Charts pick themselves better.** The agent now checks the chart against a proven matrix before drawing ‚Äî a pie with too many slices becomes a bar, a time series shown as bars becomes a line, and so on ‚Äî so you get the right chart for the message instead of a cluttered one.
  - **Every agent profiles its own data.** On training (or on demand from the agent's Overview), each agent now shows a "Data at a glance" first-look: what's in the data, the top categories, the peak period, outliers, a few plain-language insights, and suggested first questions to ask. It's saved per agent and shown only on that agent's screen.
  - Foundation shipped: 7 BI-uplift flags (3-place in `hybrid_flags.py`), migration `biuplift1` (`data_sources.eda_profile` + `kpi_defs` JSON), shared deterministic `services/analytics/compute.py` (profile / missing-data plan / signal sweep / correlations ‚Äî pure pandas, no LLM). Phase 1 = `chart_guardrail.py` wired into `create_data` (flag `HYBRID_CHART_GUARDRAIL`). Phase 6 = `agent_eda.py` (compute-then-narrate: bounded sample ‚Üí computed profile ‚Üí LLM insights grounded ONLY on the numbers ‚Üí persist), `auto_eda` train stage, `POST /data_sources/{id}/auto-eda` on-demand rebuild, `eda_profile` on `DataSourceSchema`, render in `components/AgentDetail.vue` Overview (flag `HYBRID_AUTO_EDA`). Verified live on a 5,000√ó41 agent (5 grounded insights + 4 questions). Compute-then-narrate + fail-soft throughout. Remaining phases (insight-engine, KPI layer, dashboard composer, LLM-driven methods) scoped and flag-stubbed for follow-up bakes.

Fix = root `h-dvh` ‚Üí `h-full` (fill the already-bounded parent). One-line, no logic change.

## v1.92.0 ‚Äî Agents ship with a filled Overview (primary instruction + starters)  (2026-07-05)
- A freshly-trained agent no longer shows a blank Overview. When training finishes, if the agent has no primary instruction it gets one pinned (an existing high-level instruction, or a clean auto-written one), and if it has no conversation starters a few useful ones are added ‚Äî so the panel and the report's starter chips are populated out of the box. Only fills what's missing; your own choices are never overwritten.
  - Root cause: the Overview panel reads two dedicated `data_sources` columns ‚Äî `primary_instruction_id` and `conversation_starters` ‚Äî that the training pipeline never populated (the Instructions-tab count is a different source; the report's chips were a frontend-only generic fallback). Fresh agents therefore read "No primary instruction / No conversation starters".
  - NEW `backend/app/services/knowledge/agent_overview.py::autofill_agent_overview` ‚Äî pins the best existing non-guardrail instruction (prefers general/overview/definition/semantic/business categories) or synthesizes+links a 1-paragraph primary from the agent name; seeds 4 default starters. Fail-soft, commits only when something changed.
  - Wired as a new fail-soft `agent_overview` stage (pct 99, before Done) in `ai/knowledge/train_orchestrator.py`, iterating the studio's sources. Flag `HYBRID_AUTOFILL_AGENT_OVERVIEW` (3-place in `settings/hybrid_flags.py`, default ON). Verified: blank throwaway agent ‚Üí 4 starters + synthesized pinned primary; already-populated agents ‚Üí no-op.

  - **Mobile** ‚Äî NEW `frontend/assets/css/mobile.css` (16px min input font <640px + `overflow-x:hidden`/`max-width:100vw`) registered in `nuxt.config.ts`; `composables/useSidebar.ts` `mobileOpen`/`openMobile`/`closeMobile`/`toggleMobile` (upstream API parity ‚Äî our mobile nav drawer already lives in `nav/TopNav.vue`); `layouts/default.vue` app-shell `h-screen`‚Üí`h-dvh`; per-component: `AgGridComponent.vue` (flex/minWidth cols + pagination only when rows>50), `RenderTable.vue` (paging panel wraps), `dashboard/charts/EChartsVisual.vue` (`hideOverlap:true` for ‚â§5 categories), `prompt/PromptBoxV2.vue` + `report/SplitScreenLayout.vue` (`h-dvh`) + `reports/[id]/index.vue` + `r/[id]/index.vue` mobile spacing; `useHead` report-title tab name on both `reports/[id]` and public `r/[id]` (public top bar goes icon-only on mobile).

## v1.87.0 ‚Äî Dash-inspired hardening: safety evals ¬∑ read-only ¬∑ materialize ¬∑ gotchas ¬∑ remember  (2026-07-03)
- Five upgrades borrowed from the agno-agi/dash self-learning agent, all off by default (Settings ‚Üí Features):
  - **Safety & reliability evals** ‚Äî beyond "is the number right", the agent's answers are now judged for four safety checks: no secret/credential leak, refuses destructive SQL, stays inside its own data (verifies the Shared-Memory isolation), and picks the right tool. Clear violations fail-closed instantly; infra hiccups never block. Flag HYBRID_SAFETY_EVALS.
  - **Structural read-only** ‚Äî the agent's query connection is opened read-only at the database level (Postgres `default_transaction_read_only=on`), so even a prompt-injection can't DROP/DELETE/ALTER your source data ‚Äî enforced by the DB, not a prompt. Flag HYBRID_READONLY_ENFORCE.
  - **Materialize hot metrics** ‚Äî query patterns reused enough surface as "asset candidates" you can turn into a fast pre-computed view (relational sources; Power BI DAX served from cache). Flag HYBRID_ASSET_MATERIALIZE.
  - **Data gotchas ‚Üí global memory** ‚Äî quality traps found at ingest (a text column that's really a number, near-duplicate categories) are written to Global memory so every agent avoids them. Flag HYBRID_GOTCHA_MEMORY.
  - **Remember this** ‚Äî the agent can now explicitly save a proven query/approach to Shared Memory mid-answer, not only via the automatic gate. Reuses Shared Memory.
  - Backend: `services/evals/safety_evals.py` (4 LLM-judges + deterministic fail-closed on secrets/destructive-SQL, wired into `eval_harness.save_completion_as_golden`); `postgresql_client` read-only conn + `code_execution` structural guard (flag-gated) + `data_source_service` agent-path client; `services/knowledge/materialize.py` + `GET /api/memory/hot-assets`; `services/knowledge_gotchas.py` ‚Üí `capture_global`, wired `ingest/post_ingest.py:557`; `ai/tools/implementations/remember_this.py` (+ schema, auto-registers ‚Üí 45 tools). 4 new flags (3-place). Built via 4 parallel subagents + inline materialize. All flag-gated + fail-soft; OFF = byte-identical.

## v1.86.0 ‚Äî Shared Memory: global tier + mistake learning + tiered views  (2026-07-03)
- Shared Memory grows up. Three clear tiers now: **Global** (every agent learns from it ‚Äî house rules, universal fixes), **By data** (shared with anyone who has the same data source), and **Personal** (private to you). Agents now also learn from *fixed mistakes* automatically ‚Äî when a query errors and a later attempt works, the fix is remembered so it isn't repeated. When an answer reused shared knowledge, the chat shows a small "used shared memory" chip. Admins (or the fact's creator) can remove a bad learning. Still off by default (Settings ‚Üí Features ‚Üí Shared Memory).
  - Tier-3 GLOBAL: `scope_kind='org'` (resolver `org_scope`, `capture_global`); `access.visible_scope_pairs`/`can_view` always include `('org', org_id)`; `retrieve` threads `organization_id` so every agent reads global regardless of data scope. Private tier stays isolated; data tier stays access-gated.
  - Mistake learning: `capture_mistake` wired into the live query tool `ai/tools/implementations/create_data.py` (error‚Üírecover path, flag-gated + fail-soft) ‚Äî dash-style "never repeat".
  - Provenance: completions carry a `shared_memory` field (`schemas/completion_v2_schema.py` + `services/completion_service.py`, both stream + non-stream, flag-gated fail-soft); FE chip in `pages/reports/[id]/index.vue` ("used shared memory ¬∑ <scope> (N)").
  - Tiered views: `/api/memory/shared` tags each group `tier` (global/data/personal, ordered); FE `pages/memory/shared.vue` renders 3 labeled sections; per-agent Memory tab shows tier labels. Admin curate: `DELETE`/`PATCH /api/memory/{id}` (org-admin or creator) + row Remove action.
  - Proven live: global fact visible to an agent with no matching data scope + ordered first; tiers tagged; `DELETE` soft-deletes. Built via 2 parallel subagents (mistake-hook + chip) + inline (global/views/curate).

## v1.85.0 ‚Äî Shared Memory (agents learn once, reuse safely)  (2026-07-03)
- Your agents now get smarter over time and share what they learn ‚Äî without ever sharing your data. When an agent solves something (a verified answer, a fixed error, a useful pattern), it remembers *how it was done* and reuses it next time. If two people connect the same Power BI model or database, one person's learning helps the other automatically ‚Äî but only for data you both have access to, and only the method is shared, never the actual numbers or values. Personal agents keep their memory private. See it under an agent's **Memory** tab, or all of it on the new **Shared Memory** page. Off by default; turn it on in Settings ‚Üí Features (Shared Memory).
  - New table `agent_knowledge` (mig `agentknow1` off head `colprofile1`) ‚Äî one canonical, sanitized, scoped row per learned fact, deduped on `(org, scope_kind, scope_key, kind, source_hash)`; re-learning bumps `verified_count` and promotes pending‚Üíactive at ‚â•2 (or an explicit verified capture). Flag `HYBRID_SHARED_MEMORY`, 3-place, default OFF (ON via DB override org 7d372305).
  - `services/knowledge/`: `scope_resolver` (agent ‚Üí scope keys: Power BI `datasetId` = `model`, DB = `schema` signature, upload = `file` signature, personal = private `user`); `sanitize` (leak firewall ‚Äî strips result rows / filter constants / ids / dates / emails / GUIDs; only structure + `{value}` templates travel); `access` (retrieval intersects the viewer's own scopes; private tier never crosses users); `capture` (singularize upsert + confidence gate) hooked into the verified-golden path (`routes/pipeline._save_golden`); `retrieve` (`recall_block`) injected as one synthetic instruction in `instruction_context_builder.build()`.
  - Read APIs `GET /api/data_sources/{id}/memory` (per-agent) + `GET /api/memory/shared` (org-wide, grouped by scope). FE: per-agent **Memory** tab (`pages/agents/[id]/memory.vue`, Configure group in `layouts/data.vue`) + org-wide **Shared Memory** page (`pages/memory/shared.vue` + nav item). All flag-gated + fail-soft; OFF = nothing captured or injected (byte-identical). Design doc `docs/POWERBI_LEARNING_FLOW.html`.
  - Proven: 9/9 firewall/access unit tests + DB singularize/promote/private tests; live isolation E2E ‚Äî a user sees a fact for a dataset they hold, a fact under a not-held scope is never returned.

## v1.79.2 ‚Äî No more duplicate connector agents  (2026-07-03)
- Reconnecting the same Power BI account no longer creates a second, empty agent named "‚Ä¶ (2)". Connecting now reuses your existing agent, and removing an agent fully cleans up after itself so nothing is left behind to collide with next time.
  - Root cause: deleting a per-user connector agent removed the DataSource but left its private Connection orphaned; the leftover held the base name, so the next connect hit a name clash and was forced to append " (2)". Fixes in `services/per_user_connector.py` + `services/data_source_service.py`:
    - `_conn_account_email` now also reads `ms_account_email`/`preferred_username` (the write side stamps these), so account matching can't miss.
    - `_merge_ms_identity_into_config` stores the config **dict** instead of a `json.dumps` string ‚Äî the JSON column was double-encoding (`"{...}"`), which made SQL-level `config::jsonb->>'email'` matching return null.
    - New `_find_reusable_connection` + `_strip_name_suffix`: on connect, ADOPT an existing owner-private connection for this account (matched by stamped email, or by base name ignoring any ` (N)` suffix; orphans preferred) instead of creating a new one.
    - `delete_data_source` now captures the owner-private connection(s) bound 1:1 to the deleted agent and cascade-deletes them (+ child rows) fail-soft, so no orphans accumulate. Shared / other-linked connections are never touched.
  - One-time cleanup: removed 6 dead orphaned connections + renamed 2 live connections back to their clean base name. Verified: each account now has exactly one clean agent, zero orphans, zero " (2)".

## v1.79.1 ‚Äî At-a-glance KPIs on the agent page (Hot Start, front end)  (2026-07-03)
- Opening a Power BI data agent now shows a strip of **real headline numbers** ‚Äî the model's own measures (e.g. Total Projects 258, On Risk 26, Avg Progress 82%) ‚Äî **before you type anything**, so you see live data immediately and your first question isn't the first thing that touches the model. Each KPI card is clickable ‚Äî tapping it asks the agent about that metric.
  - `pages/agents/[id]/index.vue`: "At a glance" strip driven by a `headline` ref + `fetchHeadline()` (polls while `status==='off'`/empty until ready, then stops); cards `@click="launchReport('Show me ' + kpi.label)"`. Numbers come per-user from the headline endpoint; nothing shows until the user's own client returns values (RLS-safe ‚Äî never another user's data). FE rebuilt (`nuxt generate`) + deployed.

## v1.79.0 ‚Äî Hot Start: pre-warm the model so the first query is fast  (2026-07-03)
- Power BI's first query used to take 40‚Äì84s because Microsoft has to load the semantic model into memory (cold engine). Now, when you open a Power BI agent, we quietly fire a cheap query per dataset in **your own** account to make the model hot ‚Äî so your first real question comes back fast. Fully per-user, background, fail-soft (worst case it does nothing; it never blocks the page or a query).
  - `services/connector_warm.py` (NEW): `warm_agent(ds, org, user)` ‚Äî flag `HYBRID_HOT_START` (default OFF), throttled per `(data_source, user)` (`_WARMED`, 240s TTL < the 300s DAX cache), PBI-only, builds the user's own clients, fires `EVALUATE ROW("_w", 1)` per dataset (`_warm_client`), 429-aborts the pass, `_PER_QUERY_TIMEOUT=20s`. `schedule_warm(...)` = fire-and-forget `asyncio.create_task` (never blocks the caller). `compute_headline(...)` runs the model's own measures matching `_HEADLINE_NAME` (count/total/avg/rate/%‚Ä¶), skips `usage metrics` datasets, `_fmt_value` (%/thousands), cached per `(ds, user)` 300s; `invalidate_headline(ds)` on sync.
  - `settings/hybrid_flags.py`: `HOT_START` property (`_bool("HYBRID_HOT_START", False)`) + `UPGRADE_FLAGS` label + `snapshot()` entry.
  - `routes/data_source.py`: `schedule_warm(...)` fired from the Overview handler (opening an agent warms it); new owner-gated `GET /data_sources/{id}/headline` ‚Üí `compute_headline`. Overview handler keeps the `_OVERVIEW_CACHE` from v1.78.1.
  - `services/data_source_service.py`: `construct_clients` stamps `client._bow_user_id` so the DAX cache key + warm are per-user; `_install_pbi_offline_index` also fetches model metadata (measures/relationships) so headline measures are known without a live query.
  - Proven live: `warm_agent` warmed 6 datasets in 7s; `compute_headline` returned 6 KPIs in 8.4s (cached per-user); per-user cache-key isolation verified (userA ‚âÝ userB).

## v1.78.7 ‚Äî New agents keep their business tables (relevance classifier fix)  (2026-07-03)
- Fixed: freshly-connected agents were ending up with **0 usable tables** ‚Äî the page just showed a loading skeleton and nothing to query. Now business tables (facts, dimensions) are kept automatically and only real noise (usage-telemetry, staging copies, measure-holders) is hidden.
  - `services/per_user_connector.py` (relevance step in `sync_clone_bg`): the classifier was **deactivate-only** (`if not useful and is_active: deactivate`). If the seed left a table inactive, a useful table stayed off ‚Üí 0 active. Made the classifier **authoritative**: `t.is_active = bool(useful)` for non-manual rows (activate useful + deactivate noise), with a `n_on`/`n_off` log ("N business tables kept, M noise deactivated"). Proven: deactivate-all ‚Üí re-sync ‚Üí 10 business tables (5 EDA_Toey + 5 Project Tracking) re-activated, 15 telemetry/staging/#Measure off.
  - Related (not fixed yet): a never-synced agent shows an endless skeleton instead of a "Sync now" prompt (journey-v2 = manual sync). Reconnecting the same account also still spawns duplicate empty agents in some cases. Both to address next.

## v1.78.6 ‚Äî Coder writes consistent Power BI queries (measure-first, no pandas cartesian)  (2026-07-03)
- Power BI answers are more consistent. Live testing proved the data + every query already work perfectly (count, filters, groupings, cross-table joins, and the model's own measures) ‚Äî the agent was just *inconsistent*, sometimes writing a correct DAX join and sometimes pulling two tables and merging them in pandas (which caused the giant wrong "cartesian" result). Tightened the code generator so it does the correct thing every time.
  - `ai/agents/coder/coder.py` (both prompt blocks): added a "Power BI / DAX discipline" section ‚Äî (1) DAX does ALL work (count/sum/group/filter/JOIN); Python only runs `execute_query` and returns `df`; (2) prefer a MEASURE when one answers the question (`EVALUATE ROW("v", [Measure])`); (3) combine related tables in ONE DAX query via SUMMARIZECOLUMNS/RELATED ‚Äî NEVER `pd.merge`/`pd.concat` two model tables (the cartesian cause); (4) bare table name in DAX, full `Dataset/Table` only as the 2nd arg.
  - Diagnosis (live ladder on Open Project Tracking, dataset ad16d612): 14/14 real queries PASS incl. the exact on-risk+completion join that cartesian'd before; `subjects[project_id]‚Üíprojects[id]` relationship + 17 measures (`[On Risk Projects Count]`=26, `[Total Projects]`=258, `[Average Project Progress %]`=82%) all work. Root cause = generation variance, not data/DAX/Power BI. A pre-v1.78 run (15:19) already produced a correct SUMMARIZECOLUMNS join ‚Üí capability was there, consistency wasn't.
  - Follow-up (not done): a hard dry-run/static guard against pandas cross-table merges ‚Äî deferred (executeQueries has no free validate; static detection risks false positives on legit `excel_files` merges). Prompt discipline is the safe first step.

## v1.78.5 ‚Äî Honest sync status + sync no longer crashes silently  (2026-07-03)
- The agent page no longer shows a false green "Synced & ready" while it's still syncing, and never claims "ready" when it actually kept 0 tables. You now see: live progress while syncing ‚Üí green "ready" only when tables were kept ‚Üí amber "no queryable tables found (your account may need Build permission)" when none ‚Üí red "sync didn't finish" on error. No more sitting unsure whether anything happened.
- Fixed a silent crash where a new connection would discover tables but end up empty with no explanation.
  - Backend (`services/per_user_connector.py`): `sync_clone_bg` referenced `DataSourceService` before a later function-local `import` of the same name ‚Üí `UnboundLocalError` in the learn-from-data step ‚Üí `db.rollback()` ‚Üí cascaded into a `MissingGreenlet` in `llm_sync` ‚Üí empty agent. Fixed by hoisting the import to the top of the function. Confirmed: re-sync runs clean (no UnboundLocal / greenlet errors).
  - Frontend (`components/agents/AgentSyncLog.vue` + `pages/agents/[id]/index.vue`): AgentSyncLog now emits its live `phase`; the parent gates the status strip on `syncActive` + `active_tables` so green shows only when finished AND ‚â•1 table kept, with distinct amber (0 tables / Build-permission hint) and red (error) states. On `phase==='done'` the parent refetches the overview so counts reflect the real result. FE rebuilt (`nuxt generate`) + deployed to the image.

## v1.78.3 ‚Äî Connect fix reaches the ROPC path  (2026-07-03)
- Follow-up to v1.78.2: the email+password connect path wasn't picking up the account name, so it still collided. Now fixed on that path too.
  - Root cause: `connect()` (ROPC) passes creds as `{refresh_token, tenant_id}` (no `username`) and its identity dict uses key `ms_account_email`, but the v1.78.2 `pbi_email` chain only checked `username`/`email`/`upn` ‚Üí fell back to the app-login email ‚Üí same collision. Fix: `pbi_email` now reads `ms_account_email`/`preferred_username` too, and `connect()` stamps the typed email into `ms_identity["ms_account_email"]` when the id_token omits it, so the clone is named/matched by the real account.

## v1.78.2 ‚Äî Connect Power BI by account, no more "already exists"  (2026-07-03)
- Connecting Power BI now names your agent after the Power BI account you sign in with (e.g. your email), not your City Agent login. So connecting a second, different Power BI account creates its own separate agent instead of erroring.
- Reconnecting the SAME Power BI account now just re-syncs that agent instead of showing "a connection named ‚Ä¶ already exists."
  - `services/per_user_connector.py`: `pbi_email` derived from the entered credentials / MS identity (`creds.username` ‚Üí `ms_identity.email/upn` ‚Üí app email fallback); clone + connection now named `"<template> ¬∑ <pbi_email>"`. `_existing_clone` gains a `pbi_email` filter ‚Äî matches a clone by the account email stamped on its connection config (`_conn_account_email`), with a legacy fallback matching the `¬∑ <email>` name suffix so pre-existing agents re-sync instead of colliding. Account email is now always stamped into connection config (both create + reuse paths) even for ROPC where `ms_identity` is empty.

## v1.78.1 ‚Äî Agent Overview loads fast (cached)  (2026-07-03)
- Opening a data agent is much faster, especially the second time. The Overview page used to rebuild the whole table/column summary from scratch on every open; now it's cached and only recomputes after a sync.
  - `routes/data_source.py`: module-level TTL cache (`_OVERVIEW_CACHE`, 300s, keyed by data_source+user) around `get_data_source_overview` ‚Äî the whole cost was recomputing `get_data_source_schema(include_inactive=True)` each open. Fail-open (cache error ‚Üí recompute). `invalidate_overview_cache(ds_id)` busts it; called on `sync_clone_bg` completion so a fresh sync shows immediately. Added a timing log (`overview: built ds=‚Ä¶ in Nms`). Confirmed NOT the v1.78 model-metadata fetch (that only runs on a query, never on page open ‚Äî verified in logs).

## v1.78.0 ‚Äî Power BI: no raw errors, correct joins, clear access messages  (2026-07-02)
- The agent no longer shows you raw error codes or JSON. If something fails you get a plain sentence ‚Äî e.g. "You can view this report but don't have permission to query its data ‚Äî ask the owner for Build access," or "I couldn't find that table."
- Power BI questions stop failing with "cannot find table." The agent could copy the display name (`Dataset/Table`) into the query, which Power BI rejects ‚Äî now that's fixed automatically before the query ever runs.
- Answers across two tables are correct now. The agent learns the model's real relationships and only joins tables that are actually related ‚Äî no more accidental giant wrong results from unrelated tables.
- The agent now knows the model's ready-made measures and prefers them, so numbers are right and queries are faster.
- Permission problems stop wasting your time: if you can't access a report's data, the agent says so immediately instead of retrying and failing.
  - **B1 strip-guard** (`powerbi_client._sanitize_dax`, wired at top of `execute_query`): mechanically rewrites any `Dataset/Table` qualifier inside DAX to the bare single-quoted `'Table'` (longest-first, quoted+unquoted). DAX has no dataset qualifier ‚Äî this kills "Cannot find table" at the source instead of relying on the prompt. Proven on the exact failing queries.
  - **B2 prompt** (`system_prompt`): added the bare-table-naming rule, measure-first guidance, and relationship-aware join rules ("never combine unrelated tables ‚Üí cartesian; say so instead").
  - **A metadata grounding** (`fetch_model_metadata` + `set_model_meta` + `_model_meta_prompt`, wired into `_install_pbi_offline_index`): pulls `INFO.VIEW.RELATIONSHIPS()` (join graph: from/to col, cardinality, active) + `INFO.VIEW.MEASURES()` per dataset via executeQueries (delegated-user friendly, DAX-cached, fail-soft) and renders them into the DAX prompt. Proven live on tester3: 39 relationships + 65 measures fetched.
  - **D error translator** (`_humanize_pbi_error` + `PowerBIQueryError` at the raise site; `CreateDataTool._pbi_user_message` + `error.user_message`/`terminal` in the observation; planner relay rule): every Power BI failure ‚Üí clean sentence + category (`no_access`/`auth`/`not_found`/`too_much_data`/`invalid_dax`/`throttled`); raw JSON/HTTP logged server-side only. Terminal categories (no-access/auth) stop retries. Also catches "success-with-error" HTTP-200 row/table-limit errors. SQL/DuckDB errors deliberately untouched.
  - Research-grounded (Microsoft REST docs + both official PBI MCP servers + text-to-SQL literature): DAX accepts ONLY bare table names; `INFO.VIEW.*` is the delegated-user path to types/measures/relationships; measures-as-query-surface + relationship-aware joins + error-feedback are the top error reducers.
  - Deferred to a follow-up wave: C dry-run validation, E per-user access-matrix UI, F metadata persistence (currently fetched live-cached per session) + schema-linking. Backend-only; baked `:v1.78.0`. Rollback: image + git tag `pre-pbi-semantic`.

## v1.77.0 ‚Äî Faster, more reliable Power BI answers  (2026-07-02)
- Power BI questions are faster and fail far less. Before, a simple question could take ~2 minutes, ask you two rounds of clarifying questions, and still error out. Fixed across the board.
- The agent now writes correct Power BI queries the first time. It used to make a common mistake (referencing a column without summarizing it) that Power BI rejects ‚Äî then repeat the same mistake on retry. It now knows the rule and the right patterns (count / distinct / totals / group-by).
- No more surprise dashboards. The agent no longer auto-builds a dashboard you didn't ask for.
- Fewer clarifying questions. Simple asks ("how many projects?") just get answered with a sensible default; the agent asks at most one question, only when genuinely unclear.
- Simple questions no longer get routed to the weakest model, so answers are more accurate.
- Sensitive columns (emails, staff/cashier names, account numbers) are never sampled into the agent's notes.
  - #3/#4 DAX guide (`data_sources/clients/powerbi_client.py:system_prompt`): added the scalar-column/aggregation rule, canonical patterns (`COUNTROWS`/`DISTINCTCOUNT`/`MAX`/`SUMMARIZECOLUMNS`), aggregate-at-source directive, and an explicit "single value cannot be determined ‚Üí wrap in aggregation, don't drop, don't return empty" error‚Üífix map. Coder retry fallback (`ai/agents/coder/coder.py`, both prompt blocks) changed from "drop the problematic column / return reduced df" to "aggregate it; never return empty for DAX".
  - #9 model routing (`ai/knowledge/auto_model.py` + `services/completion_service.py`): `choose_auto_model` gains a `min_tier` floor; `_report_min_tier()` returns `balanced` when the report has a Power BI / Fabric connector (join via `domain_connection`), so DAX code-gen never lands on the FAST/weak tier even for trivially-worded questions.
  - #8 planner (`ai/agents/planner/prompt_builder.py`): clarify-gate rewritten to default-and-go ‚Äî never clarify for count/list/total/"what data" asks, HARD CAP of one clarify per user request.
  - #5 auto-dashboard: `HYBRID_AUTO_ARTIFACT` override set OFF for the demo org.
  - #6 PII (`services/connector_sampler.py`): `_PII_COL` widened to `mail`/`e-mail`, `msisdn`, account-no, and person-name patterns (staff/cashier/employee/customer/full/first/last name, contact) ‚Äî WITHOUT catching bare "name" (keeps Brand/Shop/Month/project name usable).
  - Root-cause research: our Power BI client is near-identical to upstream bagofwords (same thin DAX guide ‚Üí same inherited scalar-column bug); the 40-84s tail is Microsoft's executeQueries engine, so the real levers are fewer failed round-trips (DAX guide), fewer LLM turns (planner), and a capable model (routing) ‚Äî NOT client caching (offline index already avoids the discovery fan). DAX result cache (`HYBRID_CONNECTOR_ROBUSTNESS`) already ON ‚Üí retries/repeats <1ms.
  - Deferred: #7 view-only datasets ("needs Power BI Build permission") is a Microsoft-side permission fact, to surface as a UI badge later (FE-only).
  - Backend-only + one flag; baked `cityagent-analytics:dev` + `:v1.77.0`. Rollback: image tag `pre-connector-hardening`, git tag `pre-connector-hardening`.

## v1.76.0 ‚Äî Data agents learn from your real data (no more made-up domains)  (2026-07-02)
- Data agents now describe what your data actually is. Before, a connector could be named after how you sign in (e.g. "Power BI (User Sign-in)") and the agent would invent a whole fake subject ‚Äî "sign-in logs", "authentication attempts" ‚Äî that didn't exist in your data. Fixed: the agent ignores the connector's name for meaning and reads the real tables instead.
- On connect, the agent now samples a few real rows from each table and learns the actual values (e.g. sectors "CH, CP, CV", status "On Track / Off Track"), so its summary, sample questions, and reference notes are grounded in your real data ‚Äî not guessed from a name.
- Sample questions match your data now: you get "Sales performance by location" and "Member demographics", not "Frequent sign-in failures" for data that has no sign-ins.
- Sensitive columns (identity numbers, birthdates, emails, phones) are never sampled into the agent's notes ‚Äî only ordinary business columns are.
  - Root cause: `DataSourceAgent`'s 4 generators (summary / description / conversation_starters / datasource_instruction) were fed the connector display name + a name-only schema (Power BI has no FKs / column descriptions), so weak models anchored on the name and hallucinated the domain.
  - Fix 1 (grounding, `app/ai/agents/data_source/data_source.py`): `_clean_ds_name()` strips auth-method framing ("(User Sign-in) ¬∑ email" ‚Üí "Power BI"); `_grounding_block()` injects a hard preamble + table allow-list into all 4 prompts ("name = login method, ignore for domain; reference ONLY these tables; never invent"). Upstream-parity + kills the poison-name. Proven: instruction regenerated with zero sign-in fabrication.
  - Fix 2 (learn-from-data, `app/services/connector_sampler.py`, flag `HYBRID_LEARN_FROM_DATA`, default OFF): at learn time samples `EVALUATE TOPN(8, 'Table')` per active table, records ‚â§6 example values/column into `DataSourceTable.columns[i].metadata['values']` ‚Äî which the schema renderer already surfaces as `values="‚Ä¶"`. PII column names never sampled; 429-abort; per-table timeout; fully fail-soft. Power BI only today.
  - Wired into `per_user_connector.sync_clone_bg` step 4b-2 (after relevance, before diff/llm_sync). Runs only on business-useful active tables. Beyond upstream (which stops at schema structure).
  - Proven live (agent d305b1a4, tester3): summary + starters + primary instruction all grounded ("project management + retail analytics", sectors CH/CP/CV, status On Track/Off Track sampled from real rows), 10/25 tables active (relevance), 8+ columns carry real sampled values, sign-in fabrication gone.
  - LANDMINE: Power BI TOPN returns columns as `Table[col` (pandas drops the closing bracket) ‚Äî `_strip_bracket` handles both forms. LANDMINE: flag DB overrides must use the ENV-prefixed key (`HYBRID_LEARN_FROM_DATA`); `load_overrides_from_db` only honours keys present in `UPGRADE_FLAGS`. LANDMINE: `llm_sync` writes an audit_log with `current_user.id` ‚Äî pass a real attached User (a `None`/detached user ‚Üí FK violation rolls back the whole learn).

## v1.75.0 ‚Äî Auto table relevance: only the tables that matter  (2026-07-02)
- When you connect a data source (especially Power BI), the agent now automatically sets aside tables that aren't useful for business questions ‚Äî Power BI's own "usage metrics" report-adoption telemetry, staging copies, and empty measure/system tables ‚Äî and keeps the real facts and dimensions. Fewer, sharper tables mean faster, more accurate answers.
- The agent's summary, sample questions and key-table list are now built from the useful tables only, so you stop getting "report usage" questions when you actually wanted project, sales or member insights.
- Nothing is deleted: hidden tables can be switched back on any time in the Tables tab, and your manual choice is always respected on a re-sync.
- New agents also get a built-in efficiency rule so they summarise at the source (top-N, group-by) instead of pulling whole tables.
  - New pure classifier `app/services/table_relevance.py` (`classify_table(name, columns)` ‚Üí `{role, audience, useful, reason, score}`): deterministic rules, no LLM. NOISE ‚Üí Power BI usage-metrics (dataset name `usage metrics` or `IsUsageMetricsReport*` column), `Stg_`/`_raw`/`tmp` staging, `#Measure`/`Model measures`/`Refresh Stats` + `measures` meta holders, empty/RowNumber-only tables, PBI auto date/time. USEFUL ‚Üí `Dim_*` dimensions, `Fct_/Fact_` facts, heuristic fact (metric col + dim/date col, ‚â•4 cols), small lookups, permissive default keep.
  - Wired into connector sync (`per_user_connector.sync_clone_bg`, after seed / before llm_sync) AND at the top of `DataSourceService.llm_sync` (so a re-learn re-classifies too). Writes verdict to `DataSourceTable.metadata_json['classification']` and sets `is_active = useful`; a `metadata_json.manual_active == True` marker is never auto-hidden. Idempotent + fail-soft (a failure leaves every table active).
  - Because the schema builder is `active_only=True` by default, description / conversation-starters / Key-Tables regenerate from the useful tables automatically. `llm_sync` also appends a `### Query Efficiency` block (aggregate at source: `SUMMARIZECOLUMNS`/`TOPN`/`GROUP BY`, filter early) to the generated instruction.
  - Flag `HYBRID_AUTO_TABLE_RELEVANCE` (3-place registry, default OFF, ON via override for org 7d372305). Rollback tag `pre-relevance-classifier`.
  - Verified live on Power BI agent `1b90c476` (tester3): 25 tables ‚Üí 10 useful / 15 noise (all 12 `Usage Metrics Report/*` + `Stg_Member_Account` + `#Measure` deactivated). Re-learn produced business-only starters (Top Products / Project Status / Member Demographics / Transactions), a new primary instruction with **0** telemetry mentions (was 6) + efficiency block; old telemetry instruction archived.

## v1.74.9 ‚Äî Agent Overview redesign: the agent's knowledge, front and center  (2026-07-02)
- The agent Overview is now a two-column "what this agent knows" page: a launcher to start a report, the agent's guiding instruction, its core tables (with column counts) and ‚Äî when the data has them ‚Äî the key table relationships, all in the center. A side panel shows an at-a-glance summary, any view-only datasets, and the guiding-instruction shortcut.
- Type a question in the launcher (or click a starter) and it opens a fresh report with your question pre-filled.
- Everything shown is real ‚Äî tables, joins and stats come straight from the connected data, nothing invented. Sources with no relationships simply hide that section instead of guessing.
  - New grounded endpoint `GET /api/data_sources/{id}/overview` (`routes/data_source.py`, flag `HYBRID_CONNECTOR_JOURNEY_V2`, returns `{}` when off, fail-soft): `stats{active_tables,total_columns,connections}` + active `tables[]` (sorted by centrality, cap 40, `purpose` from `metadata_json.description` or an APPROVED `SemanticTable.description`, else null) + `joins[]` from REAL `fks` (dedup, cap 30, `[]` when none) + `view_only[]` (`[]` ‚Äî no live client constructed). Reuses `get_data_source_schema(include_inactive=True)`.
  - FE `pages/agents/[id]/index.vue` re-laid-out into `flex-col lg:flex-row`: center = launcher (`launchReport()` POSTs `/reports` then `router.push(/reports/{id}?prompt=)`) + existing primary-instruction block ("What this agent knows") + Core tables + Key joins (v-if joins.length) + existing starters/edit-modal; right rail (`v-if=hasOverview`) = At-a-glance + View-only (v-if length) + Guiding-instruction CTA. `fetchOverview()` fail-soft; missing `stats` ‚Üí `hasOverview=false` degrades to launcher+instruction+starters. Layout `data.vue` already owns identity/description/New-Report/Disconnect ‚Äî not duplicated.
  - Verified live: demo clone 18 tables/165 cols, tester3 25/242, real table names, purpose null (no fabrication), joins [] (PBI carries no fks ‚Üí card hidden), view_only []. Flag ON org 7d372305.

- No-2FA accounts sign in instantly (no code screen); 2FA accounts get the code step, then the same confirm-and-consent gate.

## v1.74.7 ‚Äî Connectors: get your shared reports' data too  (2026-07-02)
- Power BI users who only have shared reports or apps (not full workspace access) now get their data synced ‚Äî before, those agents showed 0 tables even though the data was there.
- We now capture which Microsoft account you signed in with (shown on the agent), and never invent a fake schema when an account has no data.
  - Report/app-based dataset discovery (`powerbi_user_client.discover_via_reports`): enumerate reports across My Workspace + apps + groups, probe each dataset's queryability (My-Workspace scope then group scope, 429-retry), enumerate real tables/columns via INFO.VIEW.TABLES/COLUMNS (INFO.TABLES is blocked for non-admins). Flag-gated get_schemas() merge so the sync path picks it up. Capture MS id_token (openid/profile) ‚Üí ms_account_email/tenant on the connection. Skip the hallucinated overview on 0 tables. ## v1.74.6 ‚Äî Each agent sees only its own data  (2026-07-02)
- An agent no longer picks up instructions or reports that belong to a different agent in the same workspace ‚Äî it stays focused on its own data.
- Fixed the Power BI agent chasing tables from old, unrelated projects (it was reading leftover instructions that mentioned data it can't see).
  - Root cause: an instruction with NO data-source link was treated as "global" and injected into every agent's context. Org 7d372305 had 16 unscoped instructions from past projects (CRM call-center Q8-Q11 "Call Category" definitions, crypto "candle/bitcoin", CFC Fabric) leaking into the Power BI agent ‚Üí it searched for tables that don't exist there.
  - **A (data):** soft-deleted the 10 junk unscoped instructions (CRM + crypto). **B (scope):** linked the 5 Power BI overview instructions to the Power BI clone (`db1e4234`) so they only apply there; the primary was already scoped.
  - **C (rule):** `instruction_context_builder.py` ‚Äî flag `HYBRID_SCOPED_INSTRUCTIONS`: when ON, an instruction with no data-source link is NOT auto-global (applies only to its own source unless it carries an explicit `global_status`). OFF (default) = legacy (unscoped = global).
  - **D (search):** `search_reports` now, under the same flag, only surfaces reports that share a data source with the current report ‚Äî so one agent's chat can't discover another agent's reports. Fail-soft (can't resolve sources ‚Üí falls back to user+org scope).
  - Flag `HYBRID_SCOPED_INSTRUCTIONS` (default OFF, ON org 7d372305). Verified live: asking the PBI agent "what data do you have" now returns ONLY its Power BI source ‚Äî leak terms (Call Category / candle / bitcoin / conso_data / Q8-Q11) all absent.

## v1.74.5 ‚Äî Power BI questions run about twice as fast  (2026-07-02)
- Opening a Data Agent is now instant the first time (no more short stall on the first click).
- Asking a Power BI / Fabric agent a question is now roughly twice as fast ‚Äî a real query dropped from ~47s to ~26s in testing.
- Repeated or retried queries return instantly instead of re-hitting Microsoft's slow engine.
- If your sign-in quietly expires mid-session, the agent silently refreshes it and keeps working instead of failing.
- When a Fabric agent finds no tables, it now tells you why (permissions / empty warehouse) instead of showing a silent "0 tables".
  - **Root cause of the slowness (fixed):** the QUERY path built its client via `data_source_service.construct_client(s)`, which never installed the offline table‚Üí{datasetId,workspaceId} index (only `connection_service.construct_client` did). So every query fell back to a LIVE `get_schemas()` that fanned `COLUMNSTATISTICS` across every dataset (slow + 429/400 spam on empty datasets). New `_install_pbi_offline_index()` (flag `HYBRID_CONNECTOR_ROBUSTNESS`, fail-soft) is now called from BOTH `construct_client` and `construct_clients`, built from cached `ConnectionTable.metadata_json.powerbi`. A query now resolves its dataset offline and runs exactly ONE DAX. Verified live: index size=18, COLUMNSTATISTICS discovery calls 0 (was ~11), 46.7s‚Üí26.5s, answer unchanged (258 projects).
  - **DAX result cache** (`powerbi_client._dax_cache`, class-level, flag-gated, TTL 300s / 256-entry cap, keyed by tenant+workspace+dataset+max_rows+DAX): memoizes identical `executeQueries` calls ‚Üí collapses the agent's intra-completion retry loop + exact repeats to <1ms. Serves a `.copy()` so callers can't mutate the cache. Unit-verified: put-copy-isolation + TTL-expiry + size-cap.
  - **401 auto-reauth** on the DAX path (`_execute_dax_internal` ‚Üí `_reauth()`): on a 401, clears the token + re-runs `connect()` (refresh_token / client_credentials) once and retries the same query. Fail-soft ‚Äî a delegated-token-only client with no way to re-mint keeps the original 401.
  - **Fail-loud Fabric reindex** (`ms_fabric_client.get_tables`): the per-database `except: continue` and the no-accessible-DB path now log WHY (perms / 429 / empty) so a 0/0 is diagnosable instead of silent.
  - **Quieter discovery:** empty-dataset `COLUMNSTATISTICS` (`DAX Evaluate queries work only on databases which have at least one table`) drops from WARN to DEBUG.
  - All flag-gated on `HYBRID_CONNECTOR_ROBUSTNESS` (OFF = byte-identical; ON org 7d372305). Rollback image `cityagent-analytics:pre-connectorfix`. NOTE: a follow-up (question-keyed result cache in the live `create_data` tool, for sub-2s cross-session repeats) is deliberately deferred to its own verified change ‚Äî the earlier result-cache serve/store lives in `mcp/create_data.py` (`CreateDataMCPTool`, a separate MCP-server path) and never ran for agent queries.

## v1.74.4 ‚Äî Never replay a failed answer  (2026-07-02)
- If a question ever failed, asking it again now re-runs it fresh instead of showing the old error ‚Äî and a fixed answer is cached going forward.
  - `result_cache` (flag `HYBRID_RESULT_CACHE`): new `_looks_failed()` guard on BOTH `store` (refuse to persist a failed/empty result) and `lookup` (treat a legacy failure entry as a MISS + soft-delete it ‚Üí self-heals). Failure = `success is False`, non-empty `error`/`errors`, or a `formatted` block with neither columns nor rows. Conservative: ambiguous ‚Üí OK, never drops a real hit. Unit-verified 8/8.

## v1.74.3 ‚Äî Connector query reliability + Data Agents redesign  (2026-07-02)
- Redesigned the Data Agents page ‚Äî richer "Studio-style" agent cards (status, live activity, one-click Chat/Open) and a cleaner connector strip.
  - `DataAgentCard.vue` reuses the Studios `cr-*` skin (dark banner, status pill, icon badge, progress bar). Whole card clickable ‚Üí open (connected) / connect (needs sign-in). Hardcoded English microcopy (fixed the `data.ready`/`data.tables` i18n key leak ‚Äî those keys never existed in the 9 locale files).
  - `ConnectorsMsHub.vue` ‚Äî sign-in only now: removed the "Manage connectors" button + inline admin config + DRAFT/CONFIGURED chips + gear. Tiles show Connected / Sign in ‚Üí / Coming soon (unconfigured = Coming soon).
  - Connector CONFIG moved to **Settings ‚Ä∫ Connectors** (`pages/settings/connectors.vue`), gated `manage_connections` (super-admin). Nav entry added in `useAppNav.ts` + `layouts/settings.vue` under INTEGRATIONS.
  - Search box shrunk to a compact top-right field (was full-width); shows only with >1 agent.
- Agents now answer questions against live connectors (Power BI, Microsoft Fabric) reliably in one shot ‚Äî no more "couldn't find any data" or "please try again" on questions that should just work.
- Rate-limited connectors (Power BI's request cap) now retry automatically instead of failing.
  - New flag `HYBRID_CONNECTOR_ROBUSTNESS` (default OFF; ON for org 7d372305). Off = byte-identical to prior behavior.
  - **P1 auto-fill**: `create_data` ‚Äî when the model omits `tables_by_source`, resolve ALL active tables of the report's data sources instead of hard-failing "no tables matched". New `_resolve_all_active_tables` (cap 30) + caller `elif` branch in `ai/tools/implementations/create_data.py`.
  - **P2 429 backoff**: `powerbi_client._post_dax_with_retry` ‚Äî honor `Retry-After`, exp backoff 2/4/8s, 3 retries; typed `PowerBIRateLimitError` on exhaustion (clean message, not raw HTTP dump).
  - **P4 dataset-id**: root cause = `execute_query`‚Üí`get_schema()` did a LIVE `get_schemas()` re-discovery that 429'd ‚Üí "dataset_id is required". Fix = OFFLINE table‚Üí{datasetId,workspaceId} index installed at `construct_client` from cached `ConnectionTable.metadata_json.powerbi`; `execute_query` resolves IDs from it first (no live call) + single-dataset last-resort.
  - Earlier same-session schema fix (shipped here): `TablesBySource` accepts `table_names`/`table` aliases + bare-string coercion so gemini-3-flash's arg-shape guesses validate (`ai/tools/schemas/create_widget.py` + `create_data.py`).
  - Proven: 5-attempt/148s flaky PBI run ‚Üí 1-attempt clean answer (subjects 7299, projects 258, sectors 8). Deferred P3 (don't cache failed completions) ‚Üí v1.74.4.

## v1.74.2 ‚Äî Connect fix, query fix, one connector page  (2026-07-02)
- Fixed: signing in to a Microsoft source no longer fails with "check your credentials." It connects and builds your agent.
- Fixed: chats no longer error out with a technical "Invalid format specifier" message. You can ask for data again.
- Removed the duplicate "Available Connectors" page ‚Äî connect a source from the Data Agents page, one place.
  - Connect 500 (`MissingGreenlet`): per-user `connect()`/`device_code_poll()` passed the request session's `organization` ORM object into `create_connection`; by the time it read `organization.id` the object was expired ‚Üí a SYNC lazy-load on the AsyncSession ‚Üí MissingGreenlet. Fix in `services/per_user_connector.py`: build the clone in a fresh `async_session_maker` session with `_register_clone_fresh_session()`, force-load + `expunge()` org/user (detached+populated ‚Üí cached scalars, no lazy-load), and offload blocking MS `requests` (`ropc_token`/`start_device_code`/`poll_device_code`) via `asyncio.to_thread`. Verified E2E: POST /connect ‚Üí 200 ‚Üí BG sync 18/18 tables ‚Üí agent ready.
  - Query crash: planner system prompt (`ai/agents/planner/prompt_builder_v3.py`) is an f-string; clarify-tool JSON examples on lines 217/223 had unescaped literal braces `{"text":‚Ä¶}` ‚Üí Python parsed `{expr:format_spec}` ‚Üí `Invalid format specifier` on EVERY turn. Doubled the braces (`{{ }}`). Verified `_build_system` renders in chat/deep/training modes.
  - Nav: removed `available-connectors` item (`composables/useAppNav.ts`) + deleted `pages/connectors/available.vue`. The `/connectors/available` API endpoint stays (Data Agents hub loads templates from it). Baked `:v1.74.2`.

## v1.74.1 ‚Äî Deleting a connector agent no longer errors  (2026-07-02)
- Fixed: deleting a Power BI / Fabric agent that had a sync log could fail. It now deletes cleanly.
  - `connector_sync_run.data_source_id` FK was NO ACTION (v1.73.0 regression) ‚Üí blocked `delete_data_source` when a sync-run row existed. Changed to `ON DELETE CASCADE` (model + mig `connsyncrun1` + live `ALTER TABLE`, verified `confdeltype='c'`). Baked `:v1.74.1`.

## v1.74.0 ‚Äî Agent auto-learns after sync (and you watch it happen)  (2026-07-02)
- After your tables sync, the agent now reads them, writes its own overview, and sets it as the primary instruction automatically ‚Äî no more empty "No primary instruction". The learning steps stream in the live log so you can watch it think.
- Cleaner log: a space before "synced", a "catalog" label where Power BI reports no row counts, and the table counter no longer overshoots (18/18, not 26/18). Plus a more alive terminal ‚Äî typewriter reveal, colored lines, a green flourish when it's ready.
  - **Instruction‚Üíprimary fix:** `sync_clone_bg` now promotes the `llm_sync` onboarding instruction ‚Üí `status="published"` + sets `data_sources.primary_instruction_id` (was left draft/unset ‚Üí empty Overview). Re-points primary on every resync so it refreshes when tables change. Verified: clone `d0c33ff1` ‚Üí primary set, published.
  - **Rich learn log:** replaced the single "generating‚Ä¶" line with real per-step `log_step(phase="learning")` lines ‚Äî reading N tables ‚Üí analyzing joins ‚Üí wrote description ‚Üí drafted N starters ‚Üí built overview ‚Üí published set-as-primary ‚Üí agent ready (results from `llm_sync`'s return, not faked).
  - **Counter dedup:** distinct `ConnectionTable` list (dedupe by name) before `set_totals` + loop ‚Üí `tables_done ‚â§ tables_total`.
  - **FE `AgentSyncLog.vue` dramatic terminal:** ported from the mockup ‚Äî warm top-glow + scanline grid on `#14110d`, per-line reveal, spinning `‚ü≥` + blinking cursor on the active line, colored tokens (table amber, rows gold, ‚úì green), and a done sequence (green flash sweep + ‚úì pop + confetti + green footer + Start-chat). Fixes: `‚Äπtable‚Ä∫ ¬∑ ‚Äπmsg‚Ä∫` separator, `¬∑ catalog` for 0-row lines, `Math.min(done,total)` cap. Baked `:v1.74.0`.

## v1.73.0 ‚Äî Live sync log inside your data agent  (2026-07-02)
- After you connect a Microsoft source, the agent opens with a live terminal that streams the sync as it happens ‚Äî each table as it's pulled, then the "learning" step, then "agent ready". No more wondering if it's stuck.
  - Connector clone build moved to a BACKGROUND task with a DB-backed, cross-worker-safe live log (`connector_sync_run` table, mig `connsyncrun1` off `peruser_tmpl1`). `per_user_connector.register_template_for_user(defer_sync=True)` returns the clone shell fast; NEW `sync_clone_bg(clone_id, org, user)` runs `refresh_schema` ‚Üí per-table log lines (`ConnectionTable.no_rows`, best-effort) ‚Üí `DataSourceService_seed` ‚Üí `llm_sync` (auto-learn), writing phases connecting‚Üísyncing‚Üílearning‚Üídone via `services/connector_sync.py` (`start_run`/`log_step`/`finish_run`, JSON log capped 300, commits each step). `connect()`/`device_code_poll()` pass `defer_sync=True`; routes schedule `sync_clone_bg` (it now owns auto-learn). NEW `GET /api/data_sources/{id}/sync-status` ‚Üí `{phase, tables_total, tables_done, rows, log[], error}`. FE `components/agents/AgentSyncLog.vue` = warm-dark `#1b1813` CLI terminal (glyph/color by level, auto-scroll, `rows¬∑tables¬∑m:ss` counter, Start-chat on done, self-hides when `{}`), explicit-imported + mounted top of `pages/agents/[id]/index.vue`; hub `onRegistered`‚Üí`/agents/{id}?sync=live`. Built via 2 parallel subagents. Baked `:v1.73.0`.

## v1.71.2 ‚Äî Fix blank clarifying-question boxes  (2026-07-01)
- When the agent asks a clarifying question, the question text now always shows (before, you sometimes saw empty answer boxes with no question).
  - Root cause: planner prompt told the model to use a `question` string, but the clarify tool schema wants `questions: [{text, options}]` ‚Üí weak models emitted plain strings ‚Üí `ClarifyTool.vue` read `q.text` = undefined ‚Üí blank boxes. Fixed in 3 layers:
  - FE `components/tools/ClarifyTool.vue`: `questions` computed normalizes each item (string ‚Üí `{text}`, object ‚Üí coerce `text`/`question`/`label`), drops empty ‚Äî never renders an unlabeled box.
  - Backend `app/ai/tools/schemas/clarify.py`: `@field_validator('questions', mode='before')` coerces strings/alt-keys ‚Üí `{text}` and drops empties before validation.
  - Backend `app/ai/agents/planner/prompt_builder_v3.py`: rewrote the "how to write a clarify call" block to match the schema ‚Äî `questions` is an array of `{text, options}`, put the question in `text`, choices in `options` (+"Other‚Ä¶"), don't embed lists in text; added a worked example.

## v1.64.0 ‚Äî Power BI: see everything you can access, anywhere  (2026-07-01)
- Sign in to Power BI with your own account and instantly see every dataset you can reach ‚Äî across your company tenant AND any partner/guest tenant ‚Äî in one merged list.
- Each dataset is now tagged "queryable" or not up front, so the agent won't try to run reports on models it can't read.
  - **#8 scan-all-tenants:** new `services/powerbi_multi_tenant_scan.py::scan_all_tenants(username,password)` ‚Üí `discover_tenants` (ARM `/tenants`) ‚Üí per-tenant `PowerBIUserClient.get_schemas()` (ThreadPool max_workers=4, fail-soft per tenant) ‚Üí tables tagged `metadata_json.powerbi.tenantId/tenantName`. Credentials-service hook `scan_all_tenants_overlay()` (flag `POWERBI_USER`, `asyncio.to_thread`) persists the merged list via the existing `DataSourceService._upsert_user_overlay`.   - **P4 brute table-discovery:** for lakehouse/warehouse models that reject `COLUMNSTATISTICS` and aren't Push datasets, `_brute_discover_tables` probes ~40 common names via `EVALUATE TOPN(1,'Name')`. HARDENED (live-test earned): skip genuinely-empty databases ("‚Ä¶at least one table" error) and abort the whole probe on first HTTP 429 (respects the 120 req/min/user cap).
  - Proven live: one identity ‚Üí 2 tenants (home City Holdings + guest City Mart Holding SG), 24 merged tables, 18 queryable / 6 not, tenant-tagged, no 429 storm. Baked `cityagent-analytics:v1.64.0` (docker commit), flag `POWERBI_USER` ON org 7d372305.

## v1.63.0 ‚Äî Training checks its own answers before shipping  (2026-07-01)
- Training now verifies each business metric against the numbers in your logic/Q&A doc BEFORE the agent uses it.
  A generated query is only kept if it reproduces the expected answer (e.g. Lead = 1,544). If it doesn't match,
  it's held back ‚Äî so the agent never learns a wrong number.
- On a real customer dataset this approved Lead (1,544), Successful Calls (7,526) and Unsuccessful Calls (4,179)
  exactly, and correctly held three definitions that don't add up yet (New User, a channel breakdown, and three
  free-form questions) for a human to review ‚Äî instead of shipping them wrong.
  - Wired the doc-driven verified-golden EVAL GATE into `ai/knowledge/train_orchestrator.run_training` as a new
    fail-soft stage (after `joins`, before `hybrid_index`), gated on `HYBRID_VERIFIED_GOLDENS` AND
    `HYBRID_FULL_PIPELINE` (both must be on; no-op otherwise). It loads `AgentDefinition`s, groups them by
    `data_source_id`, runs `services/train/golden_gen.generate_for_definitions` ‚Üí `eval_gate.evaluate`, saves only
    matches via `routes/pipeline._save_golden` (approved + `is_golden`), and HOLDS mismatches/errors. Reuses the
    existing pipeline services ‚Äî wiring only, no new logic. Detail line `verified_goldens: N approved, M held`.
  - Proven E2E in a real in-process train (org 7d372305, studio CRM): `verified_goldens: ok (3 approved, 6 held)`.
    Root-caused a false failure to the bare-python override-load landmine (`ONE_TABLE_MERGE` must be loaded from DB
    overrides for the 6 monthly files to merge into one 21,240-row table); `SpreadsheetClient` already merges
    correctly ‚Äî no client change needed. Held 3 are genuinely broken definitions (New User expected 2,025 is
    unreproducible; Channel Breakdown is a pivot mis-modeled as a scalar; Q8/Q9/Q11 are doc-format SQL errors) ‚Üí
    need business input via the instruction-driven corrector (`HYBRID_QUERY_CORRECTION`), not an auto-fix.
  - Docs: `docs/TRAINING_TODO.md` + `docs/TRAINING_STATE.md` (Phase 0 audit + proven results).

## v1.62.0 ‚Äî Honest data uploads: never silently drop a file  (2026-06-30)
- Uploading several files at once (e.g. 6 monthly reports) now tells you the truth. If some files don't load,
  you see "Only 2 of 6 loaded ‚Äî missing: Feb, Mar" instead of a green "success" that hides the gap.
- The agent stops making up missing data. When a source is incomplete, the agent is told exactly which periods
  it has ‚Äî so it answers about those and says the rest "isn't in the data" instead of inventing numbers.
- Awkward files (a title banner above the header, odd encodings) now parse instead of failing, so fewer files
  go missing in the first place.
  - New flag `HYBRID_INGEST_RECONCILE` (default OFF). Phase 1: the multi-file merge in
    `SpreadsheetClient._load_frames` records each file's outcome (loaded|failed + rows + error) on
    `last_ingest_report` instead of the old silent `except: continue`. Phase 2: `services/ingest/reconcile.py`
    `run_ingest_reconcile` compares loaded files + materialized rows vs source rows, stamps `ingest_coverage` on
    the connection config + each `DataSourceTable.metadata_json`, marks the source `degraded`; wired into BOTH the
    new-source and the same-schema-append paths in `routes/data_source_from_file.py` (append is the real
    multi-month merge path). Phase 3: `tables_schema_section._render_coverage_note` injects a hard DATA COVERAGE
    warning into the planner schema for a degraded source. Phase 4: the reconcile flag also enables the robust
    readers (`csv_reader`/`excel_reader`) so banner/odd-format files parse. Phase 5: `UploadSpreadsheetModal.vue`
    shows a red persistent warning naming the missing files. Row-shortfall check ignores no_rows==0 (DuckDB tables
    report 0) to avoid false-degrade. No migration; off = byte-identical to today.

## v1.61.0 ‚Äî Full-deployment default: everything fail-soft ON  (2026-06-28)
- Every feature that can't crash, lose data, or block users is now ON out of the box ‚Äî the intended posture for
  a full engineer install. 16 more flipped: Auto-configure-from-Doc, Code Enrich, Hybrid Search, File Browser,
  Scheduled Reports, Rich Report Emails, Per-Org Quotas, Pack Auto-bind, Bi-temporal Facts, LLM Context
  Compaction, Brain Graph, DuckDB Federation, and the 4 daemons (Insight, Eval, Join-Mining, Studio-Learn).
  - `hybrid_flags.py` `_bool(...,True)` flips for all of the above. All are fail-soft: no-op without their
    prerequisite (SMTP/OAuth/S3/entities/index), cost-only when used, or behavior-transparent. Verified: all-on
    boot is clean (health 200, zero errors), all 5 daemons register, `import main` OK.
  - **HELD OFF (the one genuine footgun): `HYBRID_AUTOTRAIN_ON_INDEX`** ‚Äî auto-trains EVERY table when a
    connector is indexed ‚Üí runaway token/time cost on a large warehouse. Enable per-deployment only when wanted.
  - Quotas default-ON is safe: fail-open with no UsagePolicy (always allows) until a policy is configured.
  - Daemons start at the install restart; infra-gated features (File Browser/OAuth, Reports/SMTP, Federation/S3)
    surface but no-op until the engineer wires the backend. Re-baked + tagged `v1.61.0`.
  - Net OFF now: only AUTOTRAIN_ON_INDEX + the 6 retired skill/subagent flags (hidden).
